<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 超参数迁移已成为现代大规模训练方案的重要组成部分。现有方法（如muP）主要关注模型尺寸间的迁移，而跨批次大小与训练时长的迁移通常依赖于基于时间尺度保持、二次代理模型和连续时间近似等洞见得出的经验缩放规则。本研究通过基于线性最小化预言机（LMO）方法的最新收敛界视角，探究现代一阶优化器的超参数缩放规律——该框架涵盖归一化SGD、signSGD（近似Adam）及Muon等优化器。将近期文献中的收敛界作为代理目标，并在不同调参机制下对其进行最小化，我们推导出学习率、动量与批次大小随迭代次数或计算令牌预算变化的闭式幂律调度方案。在固定模型尺寸的前提下，我们的分析以统一且原则性的视角复现了文献中的多数洞见与观测结果，并为未来研究指明了清晰方向。研究结果特别关注动量与批次大小缩放间的交互作用，表明多种缩放策略的组合可能实现最优性能。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Hyperparameter transfer has become an important component of modern large-scale training recipes. Existing methods, such as muP, primarily focus on transfer between model sizes, with transfer across batch sizes and training horizons often relying on empirical scaling rules informed by insights from timescale preservation, quadratic proxies, and continuous-time approximations. We study hyperparameter scaling laws for modern first-order optimizers through the lens of recent convergence bounds for methods based on the Linear Minimization Oracle (LMO), a framework that includes normalized SGD, signSGD (approximating Adam), and Muon. Treating bounds in recent literature as a proxy and minimizing them across different tuning regimes yields closed-form power-law schedules for learning rate, momentum, and batch size as functions of the iteration or token budget. Our analysis, holding model size fixed, recovers most insights and observations from the literature under a unified and principled perspective, with clear directions open for future research. Our results draw particular attention to the interaction between momentum and batch-size scaling, suggesting that optimal performance may be achieved with several scaling strategies.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: hyperparameter scaling laws, modern optimization theory, Linear Minimization Oracle (LMO), first-order optimizers, learning rate scheduling, momentum scaling, batch size scaling, convergence bounds

---

### 195. ❌ GASP: Guided Asymmetric Self-Play For Coding LLMs

**作者**: Swadesh Jana, Cansu Sancaktar, Tomáš Daniš, Georg Martius, Antonio Orvieto, Pavel Kolev
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-16
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15957v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15957v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

|------|------|------|------|

**评分理由**: 论文《GASP: Guided Asymmetric Self-Play For Coding LLMs》的研究内容完全聚焦于大型语言模型（LLMs）的后训练方法，特别是针对编程代码生成任务的非对称自博弈技术。论文的核心是提出一种引导式非对称自博弈框架，以改进模型在编程基准测试（如LiveCodeBench）上的性能。所有给定的评分关键词均与医学影像分析、临床决策支持、疾病诊断/预后、手术规划等医疗AI领域直接相关，而本论文的研究领域是自然语言处理/代码生成，与医疗影像无任何关联。因此，所有关键词的相关度评分均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文针对代码生成大型语言模型的后训练，提出了一种引导式非对称自博弈方法（GASP），通过基于真实数据目标问题构建课程，显著提升了模型在编程基准测试上的性能，并解决了此前方法中难题缺乏针对性的问题。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 非对称自我博弈已成为大语言模型后训练的一种新兴范式，其中教师模型持续生成问题供学生模型在其学习能力边界进行求解。尽管这类方法有望实现无需人类数据的开放式数据生成自举，但它们存在一个主要缺陷：并非所有难以解决的问题都具有提升模型整体能力所需的趣味性或信息量。当前的非对称自我博弈方法缺乏目标导向，不具备真实基础。我们提出导向型非对称自我博弈（Guided Asymmetric Self-Play, GASP），该方法通过真实数据中的目标标杆问题提供基础支撑——这些被识别为对模型构成艰难探索挑战的问题。在自我博弈过程中，教师模型首先生成一个困难问题的简化变体，随后生成该简化问题的更难变体，旨在通过训练逐步缩小与目标标杆之间的差距。通过这种方式，我们在LiveCodeBench（LCB）上的pass@20指标比无导向非对称自我博弈提升了2.5%，并借助教师构建的课程体系，成功解决了所有基线模型均无法攻克的困难目标标杆问题。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Asymmetric self-play has emerged as a promising paradigm for post-training large language models, where a teacher continually generates questions for a student to solve at the edge of the student's learnability. Although these methods promise open-ended data generation bootstrapped from no human data, they suffer from one major problem: not all problems that are hard to solve are interesting or informative to improve the overall capabilities of the model. Current asymmetric self-play methods are goal-agnostic with no real grounding. We propose Guided Asymmetric Self-Play (GASP), where grounding is provided by real-data goalpost questions that are identified to pose a hard exploration challenge to the model. During self-play, the teacher first generates an easier variant of a hard question, and then a harder variant of that easier question, with the goal of gradually closing the gap to the goalpost throughout training. Doing so, we improve pass@20 on LiveCodeBench (LCB) by 2.5% over unguided asymmetric self-play, and through the curriculum constructed by the teacher, we manage to solve hard goalpost questions that remain out of reach for all baselines.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: asymmetric self-play, large language models, post-training, code generation, guided learning, curriculum learning, LiveCodeBench, goalpost questions

### 196. ❌ MobileLLM-Flash: Latency-Guided On-Device LLM Design for Industry Scale

**期刊/来源**: arxiv

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|

| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文《MobileLLM-Flash: Latency-Guided On-Device LLM Design for Industry Scale》专注于移动设备上大型语言模型（LLM）的优化设计，研究内容包括硬件在环架构搜索、延迟优化、模型压缩和高效部署，完全不涉及医学图像分析、医学图像分割、深度学习医学成像、AI诊断、预后预测、手术规划、多模态医学成像或医学成像基础模型等医疗领域主题。所有关键词与论文内容完全无关。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种在移动延迟约束下通过硬件在环架构搜索设计高效部署的移动设备大型语言模型的方法，并开发了MobileLLM-Flash模型系列，在移动CPU上实现了更快的预填充和解码速度，同时保持或提升模型质量。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 实时人工智能体验要求针对资源受限硬件进行高效部署优化的设备端大语言模型（On-Device Large Language Models, OD-LLMs）。最实用的OD-LLM需具备近实时响应能力与广泛的硬件兼容性，从而最大化用户覆盖范围。本文提出一种在移动端延迟约束下，通过硬件在环架构搜索设计此类模型的方法论。该系统适用于工业级部署：所生成的模型无需定制内核即可部署，且兼容Executorch等标准移动端运行时环境。本方法避免使用特殊注意力机制，转而采用注意力跳跃技术实现长上下文加速。
> 
> 我们的方法联合优化模型架构（层数、维度）与注意力模式。为高效评估候选架构，我们将每个架构视为预训练主干网络的剪裁版本并继承其权重，从而通过极少量持续预训练实现高精度。我们采用分阶段流程利用延迟评估的低成本特性：首先学习精确的延迟模型，随后在延迟与质量维度上搜索帕累托前沿。
> 
> 该方法产生了MobileLLM-Flash系列基础模型（3.5亿、6.5亿、14亿参数），专为高效设备端使用设计且具备强大能力，支持最高8k上下文长度。在保持相当或更优质量的前提下，MobileLLM-Flash在移动CPU上实现了最高1.8倍预填充加速和1.6倍解码加速。我们对帕累托前沿设计选择的分析为OD-LLM设计提供了可实践的原则体系。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Real-time AI experiences call for on-device large language models (OD-LLMs) optimized for efficient deployment on resource-constrained hardware. The most useful OD-LLMs produce near-real-time responses and exhibit broad hardware compatibility, maximizing user reach. We present a methodology for designing such models using hardware-in-the-loop architecture search under mobile latency constraints. This system is amenable to industry-scale deployment: it generates models deployable without custom kernels and compatible with standard mobile runtimes like Executorch. Our methodology avoids specialized attention mechanisms and instead uses attention skipping for long-context acceleration.
>   Our approach jointly optimizes model architecture (layers, dimensions) and attention pattern. To efficiently evaluate candidates, we treat each as a pruned version of a pretrained backbone with inherited weights, thereby achieving high accuracy with minimal continued pretraining. We leverage the low cost of latency evaluation in a staged process: learning an accurate latency model first, then searching for the Pareto-frontier across latency and quality.
>   This yields MobileLLM-Flash, a family of foundation models (350M, 650M, 1.4B) for efficient on-device use with strong capabilities, supporting up to 8k context length. MobileLLM-Flash delivers up to 1.8x and 1.6x faster prefill and decode on mobile CPUs with comparable or superior quality. Our analysis of Pareto-frontier design choices offers actionable principles for OD-LLM design.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: on-device large language models, hardware-in-the-loop architecture search, mobile latency constraints, attention skipping, pruned pretrained backbone, Pareto-frontier optimization, foundation models, Executorch compatibility

### 197. ❌ Efficient Shadow Tomography of Thermal States

**作者**: Chi-Fang Chen, András Gilyén
**期刊/来源**: arxiv

**评分理由**: 论文《Efficient Shadow Tomography of Thermal States》研究量子计算中的热态影子层析技术，涉及量子态估计、哈密顿量模拟和量子算法优化。所有评分关键词均聚焦于医学影像分析、深度学习医疗应用、疾病诊断/预后、手术规划等临床医学领域。该论文属于基础量子计算理论，与医学影像或临床决策支持无任何直接关联，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种高效的量子协议，用于从吉布斯态中估计多个可观测量，通过将量子吉布斯采样器解释为细致平衡测量通道，显著降低了量子热模拟中的读出成本。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们提出一种通用协议，仅需吉布斯态的 $\mathcal{O}(\log (M)/\varepsilon^2)$ 份副本即可估计 $M$ 个可观测量，且该吉布斯态的哈密顿量可被访问。该协议采用单副本、非自适应测量，总哈密顿量模拟时间为 $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(βM/\varepsilon^2)$；我们证明，在禁止指数时间哈密顿量模拟的黑盒设定下，该样本复杂度是最优的。其核心思想是对量子吉布斯采样器的一种新诠释：将其视为\textit{细致平衡测量通道}——即在结果被边缘化时能保持吉布斯态的测量通道。因此，当哈密顿量已知时，热态的阴影层析成像存在一种通用高效算法，从而大幅降低了量子热模拟的读出成本。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We present a general protocol for estimating $M$ observables from only $\mathcal{O}(\log (M)/\varepsilon^2)$ copies of a Gibbs state whose Hamiltonian is accessible. The protocol uses single-copy, nonadaptive measurements and uses a total Hamiltonian simulation time of $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(βM/\varepsilon^2)$; we show that the sample complexity is optimal in a black-box setting where exponential time Hamiltonian simulation is prohibited. The key idea is a new interpretation of quantum Gibbs samplers as \textit{detailed-balance measurement channels}: measurements that preserve the Gibbs state when outcomes are marginalized. Consequently, shadow tomography of thermal states admits a general efficient algorithm when the Hamiltonian is known, substantially lowering the readout cost in quantum thermal simulation.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: shadow tomography, thermal states, Gibbs state, Hamiltonian simulation, quantum algorithms, measurement channels, sample complexity, quantum thermal simulation

### 198. ❌ Measurement-Based Estimation of Causal Conditional Variances and Its Application to Macroscopic quantum phenomenon

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究基于测量记录的量子估计方法，应用于宏观量子纠缠和压缩态生成，并分析其重建偏差的可忽略条件。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们在C.Meng等人（《科学进展》8, 7585 (2022)）所建立的理论框架基础上，对一种基于失谐腔系统中机械振子的量子估计方法进行了分析研究，该方法仅依赖于零差测量记录。仅基于测量记录的估计具有重要意义，因为它能在无需假设真实系统状态知识的前提下实现量子态验证。我们通过因果与反因果量子维纳滤波器构建了一个相对估计算符，并计算了其方差。将结果与因果条件方差之间的偏差定义为重构偏差，并通过解析方法评估了其大小。研究表明，在典型量子态制备实验相关的参数范围内，重构偏差足够小，可以忽略不计。作为量子态验证的应用示例，我们将该方法应用于两项提案：一是电磁相互作用介导的宏观量子纠缠方案，二是通过零差测量产生的条件动量压缩态方案；进而明确了重构偏差可忽略的条件，以及偏差变得显著的情形。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We analytically investigate a quantum estimation method for a mechanical oscillator in a detuned cavity system based solely on homodyne measurement records, building on the framework developed by C.Meng et al. (Science Advances 8, 7585 (2022)). Estimation based only on measurement records is important because it enables state verification without assuming knowledge of the true system state. We construct a relative estimate operator from causal and anti-causal quantum Wiener filters and calculate its variance. The deviation from the causal conditional variance is defined as a reconstruction bias, whose magnitude is evaluated analytically. We show that, within experimentally relevant parameter regimes for typical quantum-state preparation, the reconstruction bias is sufficiently small to be neglected. As applications to state verification, we apply the method to proposals for macroscopic quantum entanglement mediated by electromagnetic interactions and for conditional momentum-squeezed states generated by homodyne detection, and clarify the conditions under which the bias remains negligible and when the reconstruction bias becomes significant.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum estimation, homodyne measurement, causal conditional variance, macroscopic quantum entanglement, quantum Wiener filters, reconstruction bias, state verification, mechanical oscillator

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了具有对称性的不可约自由费米子系统中的拓扑K理论谱实现，并证明了十重分类对弱相互作用具有稳定性。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们基于具有对称性的不可约自由费米子系统的时间演化算子，提出了拓扑K理论谱$KU$与$KO$的具体实现，并给出了结构悬垂映射的显式公式。同时，我们引入了弱相互作用时间演化算子的几何定义，并证明了由此关联的谱$KU^{wi}$与$KO^{wi}$可通过形变收缩到$KU$与$KO$。由此，我们通过稳定同伦理论证明了“十重分类”对于弱相互作用具有稳定性。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We present implementations of the topological K-theory spectra $KU$ and $KO$ in terms of time evolution operators of irreducible free fermion systems with symmetries, with explicit formulas for the structural suspension maps. We also introduce a geometric definition of weakly interacting time evolution operators, and show how associated spectra $KU^{wi}$ and $KO^{wi}$ deformation retract to $KU$ and $KO$. We thus have a stable homotopy theoretical proof that the tenfold way is stable to weak interactions.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: topological K-theory, tenfold way, free fermion systems, symmetries, time evolution operators, stable homotopy theory, weak interactions, KU and KO spectra

### 200. ❌ Boosted linear-optical measurements on single-rail qubits with unentangled ancillas

**作者**: Aqil Sajjad, Isack Padilla, Saikat Guha
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16795v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16795v1)

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文解决了单轨量子比特在缺乏强非线性时难以进行任意测量的问题，通过使用非纠缠辅助量子比特、8端口干涉仪和光子检测，实现了在XY布洛赫平面上任意单轨量子比特测量，成功概率达到147/256，超越了先前已知的1/2极限。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 辐射场的任意量子态在非重叠的时空单元中切片后，均可视为一系列单轨量子比特的集合，每个量子比特跨越一个模式的真空态与单光子福克态。对这些量子比特进行量子逻辑操作将能实现对承载信息的光场进行任意测量，但由于缺乏强非线性相互作用，这一目标难以实现。通过使用非纠缠的辅助单轨量子比特、一个$8$端口干涉仪以及光子探测技术，我们证明在$XY$布洛赫平面上的任何单轨量子比特测量均能以$147/256$的成功概率实现，该概率超越了此前已知的$1/2$极限。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Any quantum state of the radiation field, sliced in small non-overlapping space-time bins is a collection of single-rail qubits, each spanning the vacuum and single-photon Fock state of a mode. Quantum logic on these qubits would enable arbitrary measurements on information-bearing light, but is hard due to the lack of strong nonlinearities. With unentangled ancilla single-rail qubits, an $8$-port interferometer and photon detection, we show any single-rail qubit measurement in the $XY$ Bloch plane is realizable with success probability $147/256$, which beats the prior-known $1/2$ limit.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: single-rail qubits, quantum measurement, interferometer, photon detection, Bloch plane, quantum optics, success probability

### 201. ❌ Quantum signal processing in Hilbert space fragmented systems

**作者**: Naoya Egawa, Kaoru Mizuta, Joji Nasu
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16784v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16784v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| medical image segmentation | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究量子信号处理在希尔伯特空间碎片化系统中的应用，属于量子物理和量子计算领域，与医学图像分析、人工智能临床决策支持等医疗领域完全无关。论文未涉及任何医学图像、深度学习、疾病诊断、手术规划或多模态医疗数据相关内容。

<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了如何将量子信号处理扩展到非可积系统，通过利用希尔伯特空间碎片化结构，在单个系统中实现了对可积和非可积扇区中非平衡动力学的并行控制。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 量子信号处理（Quantum Signal Processing, QSP）最初是为核磁共振系统中的复合脉冲序列而发展起来的技术，近年来作为量子算法的统一框架受到广泛关注。一项开创性研究将QSP应用于可积多体系统中的非平衡调控，实现了比弗洛凯（Floquet）工程更具灵活性的非平衡动力学。然而，将QSP扩展到不可积系统面临根本性障碍，这源于守恒量的有限性和系统热化效应。在本工作中，我们提出一种在呈现希尔伯特空间碎片化（Hilbert Space Fragmentation, HSF）的系统中利用QSP的调控方案。具体而言，我们研究了一个具有四重周期势的对跳模型，该模型展现出HSF结构，从而在单一系统中同时包含可积与不可积的子系统。我们通过解析证明，在可积子系统中，通过由这些周期势构造的QSP可以灵活设计非平衡动力学。与之对比，我们通过数值模拟在不可积子系统中发现了热化特征。值得注意的是，通过插入畴壁，我们在单一系统中实现了对多个量子动力学的并行调控。这一方法通过将QSP的适用范围拓展至不可积系统，从量子计算的角度为非平衡动力学的调控提供了新思路。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Quantum signal processing (QSP), originally developed for composite pulse sequences in nuclear magnetic resonance systems, has recently attracted attention as a unified framework for quantum algorithms. A pioneering study applied QSP to nonequilibrium control in integrable many-body systems, enabling the realization of nonequilibrium dynamics with greater flexibility than Floquet engineering. However, extending QSP to nonintegrable systems faces fundamental obstacles arising from the limited number of conserved quantities and thermalization. In this work, we propose a protocol that leverages QSP in systems exhibiting Hilbert space fragmentation (HSF). Specifically, we consider a pair-hopping model with four-fold periodic potentials that exhibits an HSF structure, thereby providing integrable and nonintegrable sectors within a single system. We analytically show that nonequilibrium dynamics can be flexibly designed through QSP engineered by these potentials in the integrable sectors. In contrast, we numerically identify signatures of thermalization in the nonintegrable sectors. Remarkably, by inserting domain walls, we achieve parallel control of multiple quantum dynamics within a single system. This approach sheds light on the control of nonequilibrium dynamics from the perspective of quantum computation by extending the scope of QSP to nonintegrable systems.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum signal processing, Hilbert space fragmentation, nonequilibrium dynamics, integrable systems, nonintegrable systems, quantum computation, pair-hopping model, parallel control

### 202. ❌ How compactness curbs entanglement growth in bosonic systems

**作者**: Stefan Aimet, Philipp Schmoll, Jens Eisert, Jörg Schmiedmayer, Spyros Sotiriadis
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16775v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16775v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<details>

|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical image segmentation | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| AI for diagnosis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是量子物理中玻色系统的纠缠熵动力学，特别是紧致性与非紧致性零模对纠缠增长的影响。所有评分关键词均涉及医学影像分析、人工智能临床决策支持等医学应用领域，而论文完全不涉及医学、影像、诊断、手术或任何医疗相关内容。论文属于理论物理和量子信息领域，与医学影像分析无任何关联。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了紧致性如何限制玻色系统中纠缠熵的增长，发现非紧致零模会导致纠缠熵对数发散，而紧致零模则能将其限制在有限值，并通过耦合振子与转子等模型验证了这一机制。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 零模，此处指约束频率为零的自由度，在玻色系统的非平衡动力学中扮演着核心角色。然而在高斯模型中，它们会导致纠缠熵出现无界的对数增长。我们证明这种发散并非零模本身的内在属性，而是特别源于非紧致零模。其非紧致的构型空间允许在位置空间中无限扩散，而其连续谱则能在动量空间中引发持续的退相干。相比之下，紧致玻色系统中的紧致零模行为则存在根本差异：扩散与退相干最终会被抑制，因此紧致性将纠缠熵限制在有限值内，使得其在零模存在时的动力学作用最为清晰。我们通过比较两个耦合谐振子与两个耦合量子转子，在一个最小化场景中展示了这一机制。随后，我们通过对比N格点紧致转子链与非紧谐振子链，证明同样的物理机制在多体系统中依然成立。最后，我们将这些认识与紧致量子场论的超冷原子实现联系起来。特别地，我们阐明了何时需要采用紧致自由玻色子（朝永-拉廷格液体）描述，以及常用的非紧致无质量克莱因-戈登模型在何种情况下失效。即使初始状态能够被非紧致高斯描述准确刻画，紧致性最终仍会主导淬火后的长时动力学，抑制纠缠增长而非允许其动力学发散。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Zero modes, understood here as degrees of freedom with vanishing confining frequency, play a central role in the nonequilibrium dynamics of bosonic systems. In Gaussian models, however, they lead to an unbounded, logarithmic growth of entanglement entropy. We show that this divergence is not an intrinsic property of zero modes themselves, but arises specifically for non-compact zero modes. Their non-compact configuration space allows unbounded spreading in position space, while their continuous spectra enable indefinite dephasing in momentum space. By contrast, compact zero modes in compact bosonic systems behave fundamentally differently: Spreading and dephasing are eventually halted, so that compactness caps the entanglement entropy at a finite value, making its dynamical role most transparent in the presence of a zero mode. We demonstrate this mechanism in a minimal setting by comparing two coupled harmonic oscillators with two coupled quantum rotors. We then show that the same physics persists in many-body systems by contrasting an N-site compact rotor chain with the non-compact harmonic chain. Finally, we relate these insights to ultra-cold-atom realizations of compact quantum field theories. In particular, we clarify when a compact free-boson (Tomonaga-Luttinger liquid) description is required and when the commonly used non-compact massless Klein-Gordon model breaks down. Even when the initial state is accurately captured by a non-compact Gaussian description, compactness ultimately governs the late-time quench dynamics, curbing entanglement growth rather than allowing a dynamical divergence.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: zero modes, entanglement entropy, compact bosonic systems, quantum dynamics, Gaussian models, ultra-cold atoms, Tomonaga-Luttinger liquid, quench dynamics

### 203. ❌ Decoherence and the Reemergence of Coherence From a Superconducting "Horizon"

**作者**: Eric J. Sung, Charles A. Stafford
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16765v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16765v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

| AI for diagnosis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是量子物理和引力物理的模拟系统，具体分析超导系统中类似黑洞视界的退相干和相干恢复现象，使用超导模拟、安德列夫反射、阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆效应等量子物理概念。所有评分关键词均涉及医学影像分析、人工智能医疗应用、疾病诊断预测等医学领域，而论文完全不涉及任何医学、影像学、临床或医疗相关内容，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了超导模拟黑洞视界系统中的量子退相干现象，发现弱耦合时安德列夫反射导致退相干，但强耦合时通过安德列夫束缚态的共振隧穿会使相干性重新出现，这为在地球上通过模拟研究黑洞量子物理提供了新途径。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 在近期发表的论文arXiv:2205.06279中，Danielson等人证明，黑洞的存在本身就会导致量子叠加态的普遍退相干（称为DSW退相干）。这一结果对量子力学与引力的相互作用具有深远意义。我们分析了黑洞事件视界的一种超导模拟系统（arXiv:1709.06154）中的退相干现象，其中安德烈夫反射（Andreev reflection）扮演着霍金辐射的角色。我们考虑了一个由阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆（Aharonov-Bohm）磁通穿过的正常金属干涉仪，其中干涉仪的一条臂通过强度可调的隧道耦合与超导体相连。在绝对零度且弱耦合条件下，我们发现干涉仪的散射态会因安德烈夫反射而发生退相干，这是邻近效应的一种非平凡表现，类似于黑洞事件视界引起的DSW退相干。然而，随着与超导体耦合强度的增加，我们观察到通过安德烈夫束缚态（Andreev bound states）的共振隧穿会使相干性重新出现。这暗示存在一种类似的引力现象：在黑洞事件视界几个康普顿波长范围内放置的干涉仪中，由虚拟霍金辐射介导的传输会导致相干性重新恢复。我们的研究结果为通过模拟系统在地球上研究黑洞量子物理开辟了新路径。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> In a recent paper arXiv:2205.06279, Danielson et al. demonstrated that the mere presence of a black hole causes universal decoherence of quantum superpositions (dubbed the DSW decoherence). This result has profound implications for the interplay of quantum mechanics and gravity. We analyze decoherence in a superconducting analogue arXiv:1709.06154 of the event horizon of a black hole, where Andreev reflection plays the role of Hawking radiation. We consider a normal metal interferometer threaded by an Aharonov-Bohm flux, where one of the arms of the interferometer is coupled to a superconductor by a tunnel coupling of varying strength. At absolute zero and for weak coupling, we find that the scattering states of the interferometer are decohered by Andreev reflection, a nontrivial manifestation of the proximity effect analogous to DSW decoherence from the event horizon of a black hole. However, for increasing coupling strength to the superconductor, we find a reemergence of coherence via resonant tunneling through Andreev bound states. This suggests the existence of an analogue gravitational phenomenon wherein transmission mediated by virtual Hawking radiation leads to a reemergence of coherence in an interferometer placed within a few Compton wavelengths of a black hole's event horizon. Our results open a new path to study black hole quantum physics on earth via analogue studies.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: decoherence, superconducting analogue, event horizon, Andreev reflection, Aharonov-Bohm flux, resonant tunneling, black hole quantum physics, coherence reemergence

### 204. ❌ High-rate quantum digital signatures over 250 km of optical fiber

**作者**: Jiemin Lin, Yongqiang Du, Mingxuan Zhang, Ruiheng Jing, Xin Liu, Xiaodong Liang, Hongbo Xie, Yanwei Li, Hua-Lei Yin, Kejin Wei
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16764v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16764v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<details>

| medical image segmentation | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究量子数字签名（QDS）系统，属于量子通信和量子密码学领域，专注于提高签名速率和抗信道损耗能力。研究背景要求的是医学图像分析和人工智能临床决策支持，包括医学图像分割、深度学习医学成像、AI诊断、预后预测、手术规划、多模态医学成像等。论文内容完全不涉及医学图像、医疗诊断、临床决策或任何医疗应用，所有关键词均与论文主题无关。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文解决了量子数字签名系统在长距离光纤通信中签名速率低和抗信道损耗能力差的问题，通过结合相位稳定偏振调制、千兆赫兹量子态编码和低时序抖动单光子探测器，实现了比现有系统高两个数量级的签名速率，并在高达49.05 dB信道损耗下保持每秒约1.25次的有效签名率。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 量子数字签名（Quantum Digital Signatures, QDS）为消息完整性、真实性与不可否认性提供了信息论安全性，是未来量子网络的基础密码学原语。尽管已取得显著进展，但QDS的实际部署一直受到签名速率有限和信道损耗容忍度低的严重制约，尤其是在长距离和城域规模的网络中。本文报道了一种高速率、抗损耗的QDS系统，同时克服了这两个关键瓶颈。我们的实现方案结合了基于萨格纳克干涉仪的固有相位稳定偏振调制、千兆赫兹速率的量子态编码以及低时间抖动的超导纳米线单光子探测器，从而能够在高重复频率下实现稳健且连续的运行。通过将该硬件平台与基于一次性通用哈希的QDS协议相结合，在可比信道损耗条件下，我们实现的签名速率较现有QDS方案提高了两个数量级以上。值得注意的是，在总信道损耗高达49.05 dB时，该系统仍能保持约每秒1.25次的有效签名速率，这是迄今报道的QDS最高损耗容忍度。这些结果为在实际量子通信网络中部署QDS建立了一条实用且可扩展的技术路径。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Quantum digital signatures (QDS) offer information-theoretic security for message integrity, authenticity, and non-repudiation, and constitute a fundamental cryptographic primitive for future quantum networks. Despite significant progress, the practical deployment of QDS has been severely constrained by limited signature rates and poor tolerance to channel loss, particularly in long-distance and metropolitan-scale networks. Here, we report a high-rate, loss-resilient QDS system that overcomes these two key bottlenecks simultaneously. Our implementation combines intrinsically phase-stable polarization modulation based on a Sagnac interferometer with gigahertz-rate quantum state encoding and low-timing-jitter superconducting nanowire single-photon detectors, enabling robust and continuous operation at high repetition frequencies. By integrating this hardware platform with a one-time universal hashing-based QDS protocol, we achieve a signature rate improvement of more than two orders of magnitude compared with existing QDS implementations under comparable channel-loss conditions. Notably, the system maintains a non-zero effective signature rate of approximately 1.25 times per second at a total channel loss of up to 49.05 dB, representing the highest loss tolerance reported for QDS to date. These results establish a practical and scalable technological pathway for deploying QDS in real-world quantum communication networks.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum digital signatures, optical fiber communication, channel loss tolerance, signature rate, quantum cryptography, single-photon detectors, quantum networks, information-theoretic security

### 205. ❌ An asymmetry lower bound on fermionic non-Gaussianity

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了费米子量子态的非高斯性度量，推导了非高斯性相对熵与粒子数分布香农熵之间的下界关系，为量化多体波函数与高斯态的差异提供了实用方法。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 费米子高斯态是多体物理学中的基本工具，它能忠实描述非相互作用的量子系统，并允许进行高效的数值模拟。给定一个多体波函数，一个有趣的问题是它与高斯态之间的差异程度，这可通过非高斯性的概念进行量化。在本工作中，我们将非高斯性的度量与粒子数分布的香农熵联系起来，该熵在纯态情况下与粒子数不对称性一致。我们基于香农熵的指数推导了非高斯性相对熵的下界，并通过数值模拟研究了大系统尺度下该下界的紧致性。我们的下界在不对称性较大时具有非平凡性，其依据是（混合）费米子高斯态的粒子数分布的集中特性。由于粒子数分布的香农熵通常易于计算或通过实验测量，我们的结果可视为一种对非高斯性进行下界估计的实用方法，同时揭示了其与粒子数不对称性之间非平凡的相互作用关系。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Fermionic Gaussian states are a fundamental tool in many-body physics, faithfully representing non-interacting quantum systems and allowing for efficient numerical simulations. Given a many-body wave function, it is therefore interesting to ask how much it differs from that of a Gaussian state, as quantified by the notion of non-Gaussianity. In this work, we relate measures of non-Gaussianity with the Shannon entropy of the particle-number distribution, coinciding with the particle-number asymmetry for pure states. We derive a lower bound on the relative entropy of non-Gaussianity in terms of the exponential of the Shannon entropy, and study numerically its tightness for large system sizes. Our bound is non-trivial for large values of the asymmetry and relies on the concentration of the particle-number distribution of (mixed) fermionic Gaussian states. Since the Shannon entropy of the particle-number distribution is often efficient to compute or experimentally measure, our results can be viewed as a practical way to lower bound non-Gaussianity, highlighting a non-trivial interplay with particle-number asymmetry.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: fermionic Gaussian states, non-Gaussianity, many-body physics, particle-number distribution, Shannon entropy, asymmetry, quantum states, lower bound

<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了量子信道的两个加性性质：一是与三明治Rényi散度相关的信道Rényi信息在α∈[1/2,1)时的加性，通过引入完全有界1→α拟范数并证明其乘性来实现；二是信道色散的加性，这与量子信息任务的二阶行为相关。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们获得了量子信道的两项新可加性结果。第一项是关于阶数为 $α∈[\frac{1}{2},1)$ 的 sandwiched Rényi 散度所对应的信道 Rényi 信息的可加性。为证明此结论，我们针对 $α∈[\frac{1}{2},1)$ 引入了完全正映射的完全有界 $1→α$ 拟范数，并证明了其具有乘性。此处推导的可加性/乘性结果扩展并补充了 Devetak 等人（Commun Math Phys 266:37-63, 2006）以及 Gupta 和 Wilde（Commun Math Phys 334:867-887, 2015）处理 $α>1$ 情形的研究。第二项结果是信道离散度（channel dispersion）的可加性，该量值与量子信息任务的二阶行为相关。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We obtain two new additivity results of quantum channels. The first one is the additivity of the channel Rényi information associated with the sandwiched Rényi divergence of order $α\in[\frac{1}{2},1)$. To prove this, we introduce the completely bounded $1\toα$ quasi-norms for completely positive maps, with $α\in[\frac{1}{2},1)$, and show that it is multiplicative. The additivity/multiplicativity derived here extends and complements the results of Devetak {\it et al} (Commun Math Phys 266:37-63, 2006) and Gupta and Wilde (Commun Math Phys 334:867-887, 2015), which deal with the case $α>1$. The second one is the additivity of the channel dispersion, which is a quantity related to the second-order behavior of quantum information tasks.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum channels, additivity, completely bounded quasi-norms, Rényi information, sandwiched Rényi divergence, channel dispersion, quantum information theory, completely positive maps

### 207. ❌ Kibble-Zurek Mechanism in the Open Quantum Rabi Model

**作者**: T. Pirozzi, G. Di Bello, V. Cataudella, C. A. Perroni, G. De Filippis

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是开放量子Rabi模型中的Kibble-Zurek机制，属于量子物理和统计力学领域，涉及非平衡相变、非马尔可夫耗散、矩阵乘积态模拟等。所有评分关键词均与医学图像分析、人工智能临床决策支持相关，而该论文完全不涉及医学、影像学、诊断或手术规划等内容，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了非马尔可夫环境中开放量子Rabi模型的Kibble-Zurek机制，发现Ohmic浴诱导了Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless相变，并且非马尔可夫记忆能够保持非平衡标度律的完整性。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 基布尔-祖雷克机制为预测非平衡相变中的缺陷形成提供了普适性框架。虽然马尔可夫耗散通常会破坏普适标度律，但非马尔可夫记忆效应的影响在很大程度上尚未得到探索。我们证明在开放量子拉比模型中，欧姆型热浴会诱导别列津斯基-科斯特利茨-索利斯相变。通过基于矩阵乘积态的数值模拟，我们发现当在冻结时间点评估时，激发能严格遵循普适的基布尔-祖雷克幂律标度。关键的是，由于环境定义了普适性类别，耗散并不天然地与绝热动力学相竞争，这与马尔可夫体系形成鲜明对比。我们的研究确立了基布尔-祖雷克机制作为开放量子系统中普适性的强有力判据，揭示了非马尔可夫记忆能够保持非平衡标度律的完整性。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> The Kibble-Zurek mechanism provides a universal framework for predicting defect formation in non-equilibrium phase transitions. While Markovian dissipation typically degrades universal scaling, the impact of non-Markovian memory remains largely unexplored. We demonstrate that an Ohmic bath induces a Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless transition in the open quantum Rabi model. Using simulations based on Matrix Product States, we show that the excitation energy strictly follows universal Kibble-Zurek power-law scaling when evaluated at the freeze-out time. Crucially, we find that since the environment defines the universality class, dissipation does not inherently compete with adiabatic dynamics, in stark contrast to Markovian regimes. Our results establish the Kibble- Zurek mechanism as a robust witness of universality in open quantum systems, revealing that non-Markovian memory preserves the integrity of non-equilibrium scaling.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: Kibble-Zurek mechanism, open quantum Rabi model, non-Markovian dissipation, Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless transition, Matrix Product States, universal scaling, non-equilibrium phase transitions, Ohmic bath

### 208. ❌ A Compact Broadband Purcell Filter for Superconducting Quantum Circuits in a 3D Flip-Chip Architecture

**作者**: Zhen Luo, Lea Richard, Ivan Tsitsilin, Anirban Bhattacharjee, Christian M. F. Schneider, Stefan Filipp, Amelie Hagelauer
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16693v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16693v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<summary>评分详情</summary>

|------|------|------|------|

| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是超导量子电路中的Purcell滤波器设计，属于量子计算硬件领域，与医疗图像分析、人工智能临床决策支持等医学领域完全无关。论文内容涉及量子比特读取、谐振器、滤波器设计、3D flip-chip架构、超导量子处理器等，没有任何医学图像、疾病诊断、手术规划或医疗AI相关内容。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文解决了超导量子电路中强耦合读取谐振器导致的量子比特Purcell衰减问题，通过设计一种紧凑的四极宽带Purcell滤波器，在3D flip-chip平台上实现了1 GHz通带和45 dB抑制，为大规模超导量子处理器提供了实用解决方案。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 快速且高保真的量子比特读取需要读取谐振器与馈线之间的强耦合。然而，这种耦合不可避免地会通过珀塞尔效应增强量子比特的衰减。为克服这一矛盾，我们提出了一种在三维倒装芯片平台上实现的四极点宽带珀塞尔滤波器。该滤波器提供了以7.68 GHz为中心、平坦的1 GHz通带，并在典型量子比特频率处实现了超过45 dB的抑制。我们通过一个测试芯片证明了该滤波器与复用读取的兼容性，该芯片集成了六个浮动读取谐振器，它们在通带内实现了强耦合。芯片采用150纳米铌（Nb）薄膜工艺制造，并在20 mK的低温测量装置中进行表征。我们还开发了一个精确捕捉滤波器响应的解析模型，该模型能直接从浮动谐振器的物理几何结构确定其谐振频率和外部品质因数，从而实现快速的电路综合与设计优化。所提出的设计结构紧凑且对制造工艺容差性强，为大规模超导量子处理器提供了一种实用的解决方案。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Fast and high-fidelity qubit readout requires strong coupling between the readout resonator and the feedline. However, such coupling unavoidably enhances qubit decay through the Purcell effect. We present a four-pole broadband Purcell filter implemented on a 3D flip-chip platform to overcome this trade-off. The filter provides a flat 1 GHz passband centered at 7.68 GHz and achieves more than 45 dB suppression at typical qubit frequencies. We demonstrate the filter's compatibility with multiplexed readout using a test chip that integrates six floating readout resonators strongly coupled within the passband. The chip is fabricated using a 150 nm Niobium (Nb) thin-film process and characterized at 20 mK in a cryogenic measurement setup. We also develop an analytical model that accurately captures the filter response and determines the resonance frequencies and external quality factors of the floating resonators directly from their physical geometry, enabling rapid circuit synthesis and design optimization. The proposed design is compact and fabrication-tolerant, making it a practical solution for large-scale superconducting quantum processors.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: Purcell filter, superconducting quantum circuits, 3D flip-chip, qubit readout, broadband filter, multiplexed readout, quantum processor, cryogenic measurement

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文通过IBM Qiskit框架模拟分析BB84、B92和E91等量子密钥分发协议，评估其在噪声、退相干和窃听等实际量子信道效应下的性能，结果表明QKD是实现量子时代安全通信的可行解决方案。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 量子计算对RSA、AES等传统密码技术构成重大威胁，这推动了对量子安全通信方法的需求。量子密钥分发（Quantum Key Distribution, QKD）基于基本量子原理提供了信息论安全性。本文利用IBM Qiskit框架，对BB84、B92和E91等经典QKD协议进行了基于仿真的分析。研究模拟了包括噪声、退相干和窃听在内的实际量子信道效应，以评估协议性能。对误码率、密钥生成速率和安全特性等关键指标进行了分析与比较。研究揭示了QKD实际部署中的挑战，如硬件限制和信道损耗，并探讨了构建可扩展、鲁棒量子通信系统的方向。结果支持了QKD作为量子时代安全通信可行解决方案的前景。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Quantum computing poses significant threats to conventional cryptographic techniques such as RSA and AES, motivating the need for quantum secure communication methods. Quantum Key Distribution (QKD) offers information theoretic security based on fundamental quantum principles. This paper presents a simulation-based analysis of well-known QKD protocols, namely BB84, B92, and E91, using the IBM Qiskit framework. Realistic quantum channel effects, including noise, decoherence, and eavesdropping, are modeled to evaluate protocol performance. Key metrics such as error rate, secret key generation, and security characteristics are analyzed and compared. The study highlights practical challenges in QKD implementation, including hardware limitations and channel losses, and discusses insights toward scalable and robust quantum communication systems. The results support the feasibility of QKD as a promising solution for secure communication in the quantum era.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: Quantum Key Distribution, QKD protocols, BB84, B92, E91, IBM Qiskit, quantum communication security, quantum cryptography

### 210. ❌ FAlCon: A unified framework for algorithmic control of quantum dot devices

**作者**: Tyler J. Kovach, Daniel Schug, Zach D. Merino, Mark Friesen, Mark A. Eriksson, Justyna P. Zwolak
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17

| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究量子点设备的算法控制框架，属于量子计算和半导体物理领域，与医学图像分析、临床决策支持、疾病诊断、手术规划等医疗AI主题完全无关。所有关键词均未在标题或摘要中出现，也没有任何间接关联。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    论文提出了一个名为FAlCon的开源软件框架，用于解决量子点设备在规模化过程中面临的设备可变性、控制栈异构性和操作模式差异等问题，通过硬件无关的领域特定语言、物理信息数据结构和可扩展测量协议库，实现了跨实验室的自动化表征和调谐工作流程。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 随着自旋量子系统规模的扩大，其搭建与控制复杂度急剧增加。在半导体量子点实验中，设备间的差异性、异构的控制电子学架构以及不同的操作模式使得跨实验室复用表征、校准与控制逻辑变得困难。我们提出了FAlCon——一个用于便携式自动化表征与调谐测量工作流的开源软件生态系统。FAlCon提供：（1）一种轻量级领域特定语言，用于以硬件无关的形式表达基于状态的调谐逻辑；（2）可传输的、融合物理知识的量子点数据结构专用库（即“调谐方言”）；（3）可扩展的共享测量协议库，支持构建互操作的实验室无关测量栈。通过将算法意图与仪器实现分离，同时保持可追溯性并支持类型化脚本编写，FAlCon使研究人员和工程师能够在异构量子点实验平台间交换、适配和部署表征与自动调谐程序。该框架支持所有用户，涵盖从使用自定义初始条件运行预置算法的终端用户，到扩展仪器支持并贡献新调谐策略的开发人员。尽管当前版本主要面向量子点实验，但其他量子比特模态及科学实验可通过提供新的调谐数据类型和仪器控制模板，复用FAlCon的模块化抽象架构。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> As spin-based quantum systems scale, their setup and control complexity increase sharply. In semiconductor quantum dot (QD) experiments, device-to-device variability, heterogeneous control-electronics stacks, and differing operational modalities make it difficult to reuse characterization, calibration, and control logic across laboratories. We present FAlCon, an open-source software ecosystem for portable, automated characterization and tuning measurement workflows. FAlCon provides (i) a lightweight domain-specific language for expressing state-based tuning logic in a hardware-agnostic form; (ii) specialized transmittable libraries of physics-informed QD data structures (``tuning vernacula''); and (iii) extensible libraries of shared measurement protocols enabling an interoperable lab-agnostic measurement stack. By separating algorithm intent from instrument realization, while preserving traceability and supporting typed scripting, FAlCon enables researchers and engineers to exchange, adapt, and deploy characterization and autotuning routines across heterogeneous QD setups. The framework supports all users, ranging from end users running prebuilt algorithms with custom initial conditions to developers extending instrumentation support and contributing new tuning strategies. Although the present release targets QD experiments, other qubit modalities and scientific experiments could reuse FAlCon's modular abstractions by providing new tuning data types and instrument control templates.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum dot devices, algorithmic control, automated characterization, tuning workflows, hardware-agnostic framework, open-source software, measurement protocols, interoperable lab-agnostic stack

---

### 211. ❌ Quantum dynamics of few-photon pulsed waveguide-QED with a single artificial atom: frequency-dependent scattering theory and time-dependent matrix product states

**作者**: Sofia Arranz Regidor, Matthew Kozma, Stephen Hughes
**期刊/来源**: arxiv

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了波导-QED系统中单个人造原子与少光子脉冲的量子散射动力学，通过对比频率相关散射理论和矩阵乘积态两种方法，分析了单光子和双光子激发下的系统动力学，并展示了矩阵乘积态方法在处理多光子激发方面的优势。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们提出了一种波导量子电动力学系统中单个人工原子（由两能级系统或量子比特构成）在脉冲少光子散射下的量子动力学研究，直接比较并对比了两种不同的量子理论模拟方法：（i）采用频率相关散射矩阵的输入-输出散射方法，以及（ii）矩阵乘积态方法，该方法使用时域量子噪声算符和张量网络技术求解整个系统的含时波导函数。从单光子和双光子福克态脉冲激发出发，我们首先展示了如何通过散射矩阵方法计算含时观测量，即利用编码脉冲频谱的频率积分，包括如何提取激发量子发射体的布居动力学以及线性和非线性贡献。我们给出了对称和手性两能级系统耦合的解决方案。随后，我们展示了如何通过矩阵乘积态方法更直接地计算量子比特和场的观测量，并得到了双时间双光子关联函数特有的鸟状形状，该形状已在近期实验中被观测到。针对单光子和双光子激发脉冲，我们对这两种方法进行了比较与对比，并显示出极好的一致性。我们还研究了线性和非线性贡献（这些贡献可通过散射理论轻松计算），并揭示了脉冲持续时间的重要作用。最后，我们通过轻松扩展至高N光子激发，展示了矩阵乘积态方法的明显优势，并给出了高达八光子福克态脉冲的示例布居动力学，其在脉冲相互作用期间表现出清晰的非线性布居振荡，类似于经典拉比振荡，但输入的是具有零电场期望值的量子场。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We present a quantum dynamical study of pulsed few-photon scattering from a single artificial atom, consisting of a two-level system (TLS) or qubit, in a waveguide QED system, directly comparing and contrasting two different quantum theoretical simulation methods: (i) an input-output scattering approach that uses frequency-dependent scattering matrices, and (ii) a matrix product states (MPS) approach, which uses quantum noise operators in time bins and a tensor network technique to solve the time-dependent waveguide function for the entire system. Beginning with pulsed excitation using one-photon and two-photon Fock state pulses, we first show how to compute time-dependent observables with the scattering matrix approach, in terms of frequency integrals that encode the pulse spectrum, including how to extract the population dynamics of the excited quantum emitter, as well as the linear and nonlinear contributions. We present solutions for both symmetric and chiral TLS coupling. We then show how to compute the qubit and field observables in a more direct way using MPS, and obtain the characteristic bird-like shape for the two-photon correlation function at two times, which has been observed in recent experiments. We compare and contrast both of these methods, for one and two-photon excitation pulses, and show excellent agreement. We also present a study of the linear and nonlinear contributions, which can easily be calculated using scattering theory, and show the important role of pulse duration. Finally, we demonstrate the clear advantages of MPS by easily going to higher N-photon excitations, and show selected example population dynamics of up to eight-photon Fock-state pulses, manifesting in clear nonlinear population oscillations during the pulse interaction, similar to classical Rabi oscillations, but with quantum input fields that have a vanishing electric field expectation value.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: waveguide-QED, artificial atom, few-photon scattering, scattering matrix, matrix product states, quantum dynamics, two-level system, photon correlation function

### 212. ❌ CryoCMOS RF multiplexer for superconducting qubit control, readout and flux biasing at millikelvin temperatures with picowatt power consumption

<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文解决了大规模低温量子系统输入输出瓶颈问题，通过开发一种在10毫开尔文温度下工作、功耗仅200皮瓦的低温CMOS射频多路复用器，实现了对超导量子比特读取、磁通偏置和驱动的多路复用，为可扩展的量子处理器控制提供了关键硬件支持。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 大规模低温量子系统受限于室温电子学与毫开尔文温级之间的输入输出瓶颈，这一问题在超导量子比特平台中尤为突出。该瓶颈在输出线路上最为尖锐，庞大且昂贵的微波组件限制了系统的可扩展性。一种具有前景的可扩展表征与测试方案是在量子比特平面上直接执行信号复用。我们展示了一种在10毫开尔文温度下工作的低温CMOS（cryoCMOS）射频复用器，其静态功耗低至200皮瓦，创下新纪录。该器件在直流至8 GHz范围内提供低于2 dB的插入损耗和高于30 dB的隔离度。直接与transmon量子比特连接对其相干时间的影响微乎其微，相干时间保持在约100微秒量级，从而能够实现读取、磁通调控以及（原则上）XY驱动线路的复用。这项工作将低温CMOS复用器确立为可扩展、高通量低温表征与测试的有力工具，并推动了面向未来大规模量子处理器的量子-经典协同集成控制技术的发展。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Large-scale cryogenic quantum systems are constrained by an input-output bottleneck between room-temperature electronics and millikelvin stages, particularly in superconducting qubit platforms. This bottleneck is most acute for output lines, where bulky and expensive microwave components limit scalability. A promising approach for scalable characterization and testing is to perform signal multiplexing directly at the qubit plane. We demonstrate a cryogenic CMOS (cryoCMOS) RF multiplexer operating at 10 millikelvin with record-low static power consumption of 200 pW. The device provides < 2 dB insertion loss and > 30 dB isolation across DC-8 GHz. Direct connection to transmon qubits marginally affects coherence times in the range of 100 microseconds, enabling multiplexing of readout, flux and, in principle, XY drive lines. This work introduces cryoCMOS multiplexers as valuable tools for scalable, high-throughput cryogenic characterization and testing, and advances co-integrated quantum-classical control for future large-scale quantum processors.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: cryogenic CMOS, RF multiplexer, superconducting qubits, millikelvin temperatures, quantum computing, low-power electronics, quantum control, cryogenic electronics

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们提出了一种基于克利福德代数与旋量表示的代数框架，用于描述两种不同的量子算法：量子分类算法和具有非均匀初始分布的量子搜索算法。在分类算法中，我们利用旋量表示的性质构建与不同类别相关联的正交量子态，并通过计算克利福德代数生成元所导出的算符的期望值来实现对项目类别的判定。在量子搜索算法中，我们考虑一个包含先验信息的数据库，其中量子预言直接通过克利福德代数的生成元实现，从而简化了其具体构建。所提出的方法为两种算法提供了统一的代数描述，均借助旋量表示来构造量子态和算符。文中同时给出了相应的计算实现。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We propose an algebraic formulation for two distinct quantum algorithms: a quantum classification algorithm and a quantum search algorithm with a non-uniform initial distribution, both based on Clifford algebras and spinorial representations. In the classification algorithm, we exploit properties of spinorial representations to construct orthogonal quantum states associated with different classes, allowing the identification of an item's class through the evaluation of expectation values of operators derived from the generators of the Clifford algebra. In the quantum search algorithm, we consider a database with prior information in which the oracle is implemented directly using generators of the Clifford algebra, simplifying its realization. The proposed approach provides a unified algebraic description for both algorithms, employing spinorial representations in the construction of quantum states and operators. Computational implementations are presented.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum classification, quantum search algorithm, Clifford algebras, spinorial representations, quantum states, expectation values, algebraic formulation, computational implementations

### 214. ❌ Logarithmic-depth quantum state preparation of polynomials

**作者**: Baptiste Claudon, Alexis Lucas, Jean-Philip Piquemal, César Feniou, Julien Zylberman
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17

**评分理由**: 论文研究量子计算中的量子态制备方法，特别是针对多项式振幅的量子态，使用对数深度电路和广义量子特征值变换等技术。所有评分关键词均涉及医学影像分析、人工智能医疗应用等医学领域，而论文完全不涉及医学、医疗或生物医学相关内容，纯粹是量子计算和量子算法的基础理论研究，因此所有关键词的相关度均为0分。

<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种使用对数深度量子电路制备多项式振幅量子态的新方法，通过改进的线性组合酉算子和广义量子特征值变换技术，实现了比传统线性深度方法更高效的量子态制备，并在离子阱量子处理器上进行了原理验证。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 量子态制备是众多量子算法中的核心基本操作，但其通常需要大量资源，目前仅对具有特定结构的态族已知高效的制备方案。本研究提出了一种制备量子态的方法，该量子态的振幅由$d$次多项式给出，所使用电路的深度随量子比特数$n$呈对数增长，且仅需$\mathcal O(n)$个辅助量子比特，这改进了先前需要线性深度电路的方法。该方案首先基于泡利基分解，构建了一个仿射对角算子的块编码，该分解仅涉及$n$项。我们引入了一种改进的酉算子线性组合（LCU）技术，以对数深度实现此分解，同时提出了一种新颖的EXACT-one预言机电路，用于标记其中恰好有一个量子比特处于$|1\rangle$态的计算基态。随后，该方法利用广义量子本征值变换（GQET）将此仿射算子提升为任意次数的多项式。文中报告了理论分析和数值模拟结果，并在一个囚禁离子量子处理器上进行了原理验证性实现，使用了$14$个量子比特和超过$500$个基本量子门。由于多项式近似在科学计算中无处不在，此方案为量子态制备提供了一种可扩展且资源高效的方法，进一步提升了量子算法在化学、物理、工程和金融等领域的潜力。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Quantum state preparation is a central primitive in many quantum algorithms, yet it is generally resource intensive, with efficient constructions known only for structured families of states. This work introduces a method for preparing quantum states whose amplitudes are given by a degree$-d$ polynomial, using circuits with logarithmic depth in the number $n$ of qubits and only $\mathcal O(n)$ ancilla qubits, improving previous approaches that required linear-depth circuits. The construction first relies on a block-encoding of an affine diagonal operator based on its Pauli-basis decomposition, which involves only $n$ terms. A modified linear-combination-of-unitaries (LCU) technique is introduced to implement this decomposition in logarithmic depth, together with a novel circuit for the EXACT-one oracle that flags basis states in which exactly one qubit is in the state $|1\rangle$. It then uses a generalized quantum eigenvalue transformation (GQET) to promote this affine operator to an arbitrary degree polynomial. Theoretical analysis and numerical simulations are reported along with a proof-of-principle implementation on a trapped-ion quantum processor using $14$ qubits and more than $500$ primitive quantum gates. Because polynomial approximations are ubiquitous in scientific computing, this construction provides a scalable and resource-efficient approach to quantum state preparation, further improving the potential of quantum algorithms in fields such as chemistry, physics, engineering, and finance.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum state preparation, logarithmic-depth circuits, polynomial amplitudes, linear-combination-of-unitaries, generalized quantum eigenvalue transformation, quantum algorithms, quantum computing, trapped-ion quantum processor

### 215. ❌ Stroboscopic detection of itinerant microwave photons

**作者**: Hanna Zeller, Lukas Danner, Max Hofheinz, Ciprian Padurariu, Joachim Ankerhold, Björn Kubala

| medical image segmentation | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| AI for diagnosis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是微波光子检测的物理实验方案，涉及约瑟夫森结、微波腔、单光子探测等量子物理和微波工程内容。所有评分关键词均属于医学影像分析和人工智能医疗领域，与论文的物理实验研究完全无关。论文未涉及任何医学影像、疾病诊断、手术规划或医疗AI模型的内容。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种基于约瑟夫森光子学器件的微波单光子探测方案，通过优化测量参数和阈值协议实现了88.5%的高探测效率与低暗计数率。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们提出了一种在单光子水平上探测行波微波辐射的新方案。利用现有的约瑟夫森光子学器件（其中两个微波腔通过直流电压偏置的超导结耦合），我们从理论上展示了如何对入射至其中一个腔体的光子实施频闪式重复、近乎投影的测量。通过对结的磁通量控制优化测量的速率、持续时间和强度，并开发阈值协议以从另一腔体辐射输出的零差测量中检测光子，我们实现了高效率、低暗计数的探测。通过将探测器与前置放大器级联（其中采用类似的双腔约瑟夫森光子学器件作为光子倍增器），我们可进一步优化器件性能，在吸收腔共振宽度$γ_a$所设定的暗计数率$\sim10^{-4} γ_a$条件下，实现$88.5\%$的探测效率。这些基于二倍增因子的结果表明，采用更高倍增因子时可能达到接近极限的效率。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We present a novel scheme to detect itinerant microwave radiation at the single photon level. Using existing Josephson-photonics devices, where two microwave cavities are coupled by a dc-voltage biased superconducting junction, we theoretically show how to implement a stroboscopically repeated, near-projective measurement of a photon impinging on one of the cavities. Optimizing rate, duration, and strength of the measurement by flux control of the junction and developing a threshold protocol to detect the photon from a homodyne measurement of the radiation output of the other cavity, we achieve highly efficient detection with low dark counts. By cascading the detector with a preamplifier, where a similar two-cavity Josephson-photonics device acts as a photon multiplier, we can further improve the device to reach a detection efficiency of $88.5 \%$ with a dark count rate of $\sim10^{-4} γ_a$, set by the resonance width $γ_a$ of the absorbing cavity. These results for a multiplication factor of two suggest that near-unity efficiencies may be reached for higher multiplication factors.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: microwave photon detection, Josephson-photonics, single photon level, stroboscopic measurement, superconducting junction, homodyne measurement, detection efficiency, dark count rate

### 216. ❌ Dark state role in time-reversal symmetry breaking

**作者**: Dario Fasone, Rita Veilande, Luigi Giannelli, Giuseppe A. Falci, Teodora Kirova, Sandro Wimberger, Thomas Zanon-Willette, Ennio Arimondo
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了量子系统中驱动相位对动力学的影响，发现暗态的存在是维持种群相位对称性的充分条件，为量子系统的鲁棒控制提供了理论指导。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 本文研究了全局驱动相位$Φ$在少能级量子系统动力学中的作用，该系统是原子、分子及固态平台相干调控的核心场景。我们特别关注具有闭环耦合的系统，其中外部驱动场会引发干涉效应，显著影响布居转移和时间演化的对称性。虽然完整的时间反演对称性要求$Φ=0,π$（对应哈密顿量为实数），但我们聚焦于一种约束较弱的变换——相位反演（或称哈密顿量复共轭变换）。在该变换下，尽管相干性通常不对称，但布居动力学仍可保持对称性。我们证明，暗态（旁观态）的存在是维持这种布居相位对称性（P$Φ$S）的充分条件，因为它将动力学约束在由SU(2)或开环SU(3)演化表征的约化子空间中。我们通过三能级和四能级系统分析了该机制，并推导出适用于一般$n$能级构型（$n$为偶数）的P$Φ$S普适条件。这些发现为在量子系统中实现鲁棒控制提供了实用指导，在量子信息处理和量子计算领域具有潜在应用价值。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We investigate the role of the global driving phase $Φ$ in the dynamics of driven few-level quantum systems, a central setting in coherent control of atomic, molecular, and solid-state platforms. In particular, we focus on systems with closed-loop couplings, where external driving fields induce interference effects that strongly influence population transfer and symmetry properties of time-evolution. While full time-reversal symmetry requires $Φ=0,π$, leading to a real Hamiltonian, we focus on a less restrictive transformation, the phase inversion (or complex conjugation of the Hamiltonian), under which population dynamics can remain symmetric even though coherences generally do not. We show that the presence of a dark (spectator) state is a sufficient condition for this population phase symmetry (P$Φ$S), as it constrains the dynamics to reduced subspaces characterized by SU(2) or open-loop SU(3) evolution. We analyze this mechanism in three- and four-level systems and derive general conditions for P$Φ$S that extend to generic $n$-level configurations, with $n$ even. These findings provide practical guidelines for achieving robust control in quantum systems, with potential applications in quantum information processing and quantum computing.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum systems, coherent control, time-reversal symmetry, dark state, population phase symmetry, driven few-level systems, quantum information processing

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文使用三维张量网络模拟立方晶格上随机伊辛模型的量子退火过程，研究退火时间与剩余能量的关系，验证了Kibble-Zurek幂律。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 采用三维张量网络模拟了立方晶格随机伊辛模型在D-Wave Advantage系统中的量子退火过程。该研究驱动哈密顿量穿越从顺磁相到自旋玻璃相的量子相变。网络以张量积态表示——在二维情形下常被称为投影纠缠对态。研究通过改变退火时间重复退火流程，以检验控制退火斜坡末端剩余能量的基布尔-祖雷克幂律。对于具有周期性最近邻随机伊辛耦合的无限晶格，采用确定性方法评估最终能量；对于具有开放边界的有限晶格，我们引入了一种更高效的蒙特卡洛采样方法。两种情形下，随着退火时间的增加，剩余能量作为退火时间的函数均趋近于基布尔-祖雷克幂律。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Quantum annealing with the D-Wave Advantage system in the random Ising model on a cubic lattice is simulated using a three-dimensional (3D) tensor network. The Hamiltonian is driven across a quantum phase transition from a paramagnetic phase to a spin-glass phase. The network is represented as a tensor product state, also known-particularly in two dimensions-as a projected entangled-pair state (PEPS). The annealing procedure is repeated for a range of annealing times in order to test the Kibble-Zurek (KZ) power law governing the residual energy at the end of the annealing ramp. For an infinite lattice with periodic nearest-neighbor random Ising couplings, the final energy is evaluated using a deterministic method. For a finite lattice with open boundaries, we introduce a more efficient Monte Carlo sampling approach. In both cases, the residual energy as a function of annealing time approaches the KZ power law as the annealing time increases.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum annealing, random Ising model, tensor network, Monte Carlo sampling, projected entangled-pair state, Kibble-Zurek power law, three-dimensional simulation

### 218. ❌ High Fidelity Single-NV Qubit Quantum State Tomography by Photoelectric Readout

**作者**: Boo Carmans, Michael Petrov, Milos Nesladek
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16502v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16502v1)

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是量子计算领域中的氮空位中心量子比特的量子态层析技术，采用光电读取方法替代传统光学读取。所有评分关键词均属于医学影像分析和人工智能在医疗决策支持中的应用范畴，而该论文完全不涉及医学、医疗影像、疾病诊断、手术规划或任何医疗相关内容。因此，所有关键词的相关度均为0分。

<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了使用光电读取方法对金刚石中单个氮空位中心进行量子态层析测量，实现了与光学测量相当的0.995保真度，证明了光电检测在基于NV的量子处理器中的价值。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 量子计算是一个快速发展的领域。然而，最常用的量子比特需要在低温条件下运行，这增加了成本并对规模化扩展构成了限制。常温固态量子比特提供了一种具有大规模应用潜力的替代方案。金刚石中的氮-空位（NV）中心是室温固态计算架构的主要候选体系之一，并已在门保真度、量子纠错、耦合等方面证明其竞争力。每个NV中心都伴有一个电子自旋，传统上通过光致发光进行读出。然而，对于构建小型、常温的基于NV中心的量子处理器而言，光学读出在收集效率、读出分辨率以及最终设备的尺寸和与标准半导体架构的集成方面引入了限制。在本工作中，我们研究了光电读出相较于传统光学读出的竞争力。具体而言，我们报道了利用光电检测对单个NV中心进行量子态层析测量。我们实现了态重构保真度为$0.995 \pm 0.0062$，与光学测量结果相当，这表明保真度并未因采用的读出方式而降低，从而凸显了光电检测对于基于NV中心的量子处理器的价值。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Quantum computing is a rapidly developing field. However, the most commonly used qubits require cryogenic conditions to operate, which increases the costs and puts constraints on the up-scaling. Ambient solid-state qubits provide an alternative with potential for large-scale application. The nitrogen-vacancy (NV) center in diamond is one of the main candidates for solid-state computing architectures at room temperature and has proven to be competitive in terms of gate fidelity, quantum error correction, couplings, etc. Each NV center has an associated electronic spin that is conventionally read out by photoluminescence. However, regarding the creation of small, ambient NV-based quantum processors, the optical readout introduces limitations on the collection efficiency and resolution of the readout as well as the size of the final device and its integration into standard semiconductor architectures. In this work, we investigate the competitiveness of the photoelectric readout versus the traditional optical readout. In particular, we report on using photoelectrical detection to perform quantum state tomography measurements on a single NV center. We achieve the fidelity $0.995 \pm 0.0062$ for state reconstruction, comparable to optical measurements, demonstrating that the fidelity does not suffer from the adapted readout, highlighting the value of photoelectric detection for NV-based quantum processors.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum computing, nitrogen-vacancy center, quantum state tomography, photoelectric readout, single NV qubit, diamond, fidelity, solid-state qubits

### 219. ❌ Distinguishing types of correlated errors in superconducting qubits

**作者**: Hannah P. Binney, H. Douglas Pinckney, Kate Azar, Patrick M. Harrington, Shantanu Jha, Mingyu Li, Jiatong Yang, Felipe Contipelli, Renée DePencier Piñero, Michael Gingras, Bethany M. Niedzielski, Hannah Stickler, Mollie E. Schwartz, Jeffrey A. Grover, Max Hays, Kyle Serniak, Joseph A. Formaggio, William D. Oliver
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16494v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16494v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

|------|------|------|------|

| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是超导量子比特中的相关错误（由辐射和机械振动引起），属于量子计算和量子物理领域，与医学图像分析、人工智能临床决策支持、深度学习医学成像、疾病诊断/预后、手术规划、多模态医学成像或医学基础模型完全无关。所有关键词均得0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种通过时域、空域和频域特征区分超导量子比特中辐射诱导和振动诱导相关错误的方法，并展示了特定器件设计对两种错误均有保护作用。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 在时间和空间上相关的超导量子比特误差会对量子纠错码构成挑战。来自宇宙及地面辐射源的射线会提高超导量子比特器件中的准粒子（QP）密度，导致QP穿越邻近约瑟夫森结（JJs）的隧穿率增加，从而引发相关误差。机械振动（例如干式稀释制冷机中脉冲管引发的振动）同样是已知的相关误差源。我们提出一种通过时域、空域和频域特征区分这两类误差的方法，从而建立基于物理机理的误差缓解策略。我们还通过加速度计数据研究了稀释制冷机振动与误差之间的相关性。我们测量了两种类型的transmon量子比特阵列：一种是约瑟夫森结两侧超导能隙差小于量子比特能量的器件，另一种是能隙差大于量子比特能量的器件（已有研究表明后者可缓解辐射诱导误差）。我们证明后一类器件同样能有效抵御振动诱导的误差。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Errors in superconducting qubits that are correlated in time and space can pose problems for quantum error correction codes. Radiation from cosmic and terrestrial sources can increase the quasiparticle (QP) density in a superconducting qubit device, resulting in an increased rate of QPs tunneling across proximal Josephson junctions (JJs) and causing correlated errors. Mechanical vibrations, such as those induced by the pulse tube in a dry dilution refrigerator, are also a known source of correlated errors. We present a method for distinguishing these two types of errors by their temporal, spatial, and frequency domain features, enabling physically motivated error-mitigation strategies. We also present accelerometer data to study the correlation between dilution refrigerator vibrations and the errors. We measure arrays of transmon qubits where the difference in superconducting gap across the JJ is less than the qubit energy, as well as those where the gap is greater than the qubit energy, which has been shown to mitigate radiation-induced errors. We show that these latter devices are also protected against vibration-induced errors.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: superconducting qubits, correlated errors, quasiparticles, radiation-induced errors, vibration-induced errors, error mitigation, Josephson junctions, transmon qubits

---

### 220. ❌ Reducing C-NOT Counts for State Preparation and Block Encoding via Diagonal Matrix Migration

**作者**: Zexian Li, Guofeng Zhang, Xiao-Ming Zhang
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16492v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16492v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical image segmentation | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| AI for diagnosis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究量子计算中的量子态制备和块编码算法优化，专注于降低C-NOT门数量，属于量子信息科学领域。所有评分关键词均涉及医学影像分析和人工智能在医疗领域的应用，与论文的量子计算主题完全无关。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种基于对角矩阵迁移的技术，用于减少量子态制备和块编码中的C-NOT门数量，显著改进了现有算法的电路复杂度。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 量子态制备与块编码是科学计算中量子算法通用且实用的输入模型。态制备与块编码的电路复杂度通常主导量子算法的端到端门复杂度。我们针对态制备与块编码提出了具有更低C-NOT门数量的算法。对于一般的$n$量子比特态，我们将Plesch-Brukner算法（2011年提出）的C-NOT门数量从$(23/24)2^n$改进至$(11/12)2^n$。对于块编码，我们针对$2^{n-1}\times 2^{n-1}$矩阵的单辅助量子比特协议采用谱范数作为次归一化，实现了C-NOT门数量的主项为$(11/48)4^n$。这一结果甚至超过了$n$量子比特酉合成所需的下界$(1/4)4^n$。针对实际应用中常见的低秩矩阵，我们进行了进一步优化。具体而言，对于秩为$K$的矩阵，我们实现了C-NOT门数量主项为$(K+(11/12))2^n$。我们的方法基于Krol等人提出的递归块-ZXZ分解，并引入了一种对角矩阵迁移技术——利用对角矩阵与绕$z$轴均匀控制旋转的可交换性，以最小化C-NOT门的使用。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Quantum state preparation and block encoding are versatile and practical input models for quantum algorithms in scientific computing. The circuit complexity of state preparation and block encoding frequently dominates the end-to-end gate complexity of quantum algorithms. We give algorithms with lower C-NOT counts for both the state preparation and block encoding. For a general $n$-qubit state, we improve the C-NOT count from Plesch-Brukner algorithm, proposed in 2011, from $(23/24)2^n$ to $(11/12)2^n$. For block encoding, our single-ancilla protocol for $2^{n-1}\times 2^{n-1}$ matrices uses the spectral norm as subnormalization and achieves a C-NOT count leading term $(11/48)4^n$. This result even exceeds the lower bound of $(1/4)4^n$ for $n$-qubit unitary synthesis. Further optimization is performed for low-rank matrices, which frequently arise in practical applications. Specifically, we achieve the C-NOT count leading term $(K+(11/12))2^n$ for a rank-$K$ matrix. Our approach builds upon the recursive block-ZXZ decomposition from Krol et al. and introduces a diagonal matrix migration technique based on the commutativity of the diagonal matrix and the uniformly controlled rotation about the $z$-axis to minimize the use of C-NOT gates.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum state preparation, block encoding, C-NOT count reduction, diagonal matrix migration, quantum algorithms, circuit complexity, recursive block-ZXZ decomposition, low-rank matrices

### 221. ❌ Achieving Sub-Zeptonewton Force Sensitivity and Spin-Motion Entanglement in Levitated Diamond via Pulsed Backaction Evasion

**作者**: Gayathrini Premawardhana, Jonathan Beaumariage, M. V. Gurudev Dutt, David Pekker, Thomas Purdy, Jacob M. Taylor

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种悬浮金刚石系统，通过脉冲反作用规避技术实现了亚zeptonewton力传感和稳健的自旋-运动纠缠，其中CPMG序列表现最佳，力灵敏度优于10^{-23} N/√Hz，并开发了考虑脉冲动力学解耦的纠缠见证协议。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们提出一种在悬浮金刚石系统中实现亚仄牛（10^-21牛）级力传感与稳健自旋-机械纠缠的方案。通过将氮空位（NV center）自旋与其宿主金刚石在磁阱中的运动相耦合，我们构建了一个旨在突破标准量子极限的平台。我们开发并比较了三种不同的脉冲序列——拉姆齐（Ramsey）、哈恩回波（Hahn echo）以及卡尔-珀塞尔-梅布姆-吉尔（CPMG）序列——以逐步增强反作用规避能力，同时抑制散粒噪声和热退相干效应。研究结果表明，CPMG序列能带来最显著的性能提升，在约10^4赫兹的宽频传感范围内，力灵敏度优于$10^{-23} \text{ N}/\sqrt{\text{Hz}}$。此外，我们推导出一种考虑脉冲动力学解耦的纠缠见证协议，证明即使自旋-运动纠缠的发生速度远快于机械振荡周期，其仍可被有效探测。这些发现为利用悬浮纳米金刚石作为高精度传感器以及用于量子力学基础检验的非经典机械系统，提供了一条更具实践性的路径。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We propose a system to achieve sub-zeptonewton force sensing and robust spin-mechanical entanglement in a levitated diamond system. By coupling a Nitrogen-Vacancy (NV) center spin to the motion of its host diamond within a magnetic trap, we develop a platform designed to surpass the standard quantum limit. We develop and compare three distinct pulse sequences--Ramsey, Hahn echo, and Carr-Purcell-Meiboom-Gill (CPMG)--to create increasing amounts of backaction evasion while mitigating the effects of shot noise and thermal decoherence. Our results show that the CPMG sequences yield the most significant performance gains, reaching a force sensitivity of better than $10^{-23} \text{ N}/\sqrt{\text{Hz}}$ for broadband sensing around $10^4 \text{ Hz}$. Furthermore, we derive an entanglement witness protocol that accounts for pulsed dynamical decoupling, proving that spin-motion entanglement remains detectable even when occurring much faster than the mechanical period. These findings provide a more practical path for using levitated nanodiamonds both as high-precision sensors and as non-classical mechanical systems for fundamental tests of quantum mechanics.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: levitated diamond, force sensitivity, spin-motion entanglement, backaction evasion, pulse sequences, quantum sensing, NV center, dynamical decoupling

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究通过光学斩波放大技术显著提高了里德堡原子超低频电场测量的灵敏度，将信噪比提升了19.1dB，扩展了传感器的检测范围。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 本研究通过光学斩波放大（OCA）技术，利用里德伯原子实现了对超低频（ULF）电场灵敏度的显著提升。传统的基于里德伯原子的超低频测量从根本上受限于1/f噪声，该噪声严重降低了测量灵敏度。我们的方法在蒸气室前使用光学斩波器对耦合激光进行调制，从而在斩波频率处诱导出周期性的里德伯激发。光电探测器（PD）的输出信号以光学斩波器信号为参考，通过锁相放大器（LIA）进行解调。这一过程通过将1/f噪声转移至可被滤除的高频波段，有效提高了信噪比（SNR）。在7 Hz频率处，OCA技术将灵敏度提升了19.1 dB，达到49.1 uV/cm/rt(Hz)。在10 Hz至1 kHz的频率范围内，灵敏度也提升了近7 dB。这种用于增强里德伯原子在超低频电场测量中灵敏度的OCA方法，使得里德伯传感器的探测范围能够覆盖从低频（LF）到超低频的整个频谱，从而显著拓宽了其应用潜力。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> This study demonstrates a significant enhancement in ultra-low-frequency (ULF) electric field sensitivity using Rydberg atoms via an optical chopping amplification (OCA) technique. Conventional Rydberg-based ULF measurements are fundamentally limited by 1/f noise, which severely degrades sensitivity. Our approach modulates the coupling laser with an optical chopper before the vapor cell, inducing periodic Rydberg excitation at the chopping frequency. The photodetector (PD) output signal is demodulated by a lock-in amplifier (LIA) using the optical chopper's signal as the reference. This process effectively improves the signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) by shifting the 1/f noise to a higher frequency band where it can be filtered out. The OCA technique enhanced sensitivity by 19.1 dB for the frequency 7 Hz, which is down to 49.1 uV/cm/rt(Hz). For the frequency range from 10Hz to 1kHz, it also enhanced nearly 7dB. This OCA method for enhancing the sensitivity of Rydberg atoms in ULF electric field measurements enables the Rydberg sensor's detection range to span the entire spectrum from low frequency (LF) to ULF, thereby significantly broadening its application potential.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: Rydberg atoms, ultra-low-frequency electric field, optical chopping amplification, sensitivity enhancement, signal-to-noise ratio, quantum sensing, 1/f noise reduction, lock-in amplifier

| AI for diagnosis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文标题为《Uncertainty Relation for Entropy and Temperature of Gibbs States》，摘要内容完全围绕量子热力学、吉布斯态、熵估计、费希尔信息、不确定性关系等理论物理和统计力学概念展开。研究领域属于量子信息、统计物理和热力学基础理论，与医学图像分析、人工智能临床决策支持、医学影像分割、疾病诊断预测、手术规划等医学应用领域没有任何关联。所有评分关键词均涉及医学影像和临床AI应用，而本文是纯理论物理研究，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究推导了吉布斯态中熵估计的量子费希尔信息，建立了熵与温度之间的普适不确定性关系，并分析了其在临界点标度和热力学几何中的应用。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们推导了吉布斯态中熵估计的量子费舍尔信息，并证明其满足 $F_s = 1/C_v$，与温度费舍尔信息 $F_S = C_v/T^2$ 构成对偶关系。二者的乘积 $F_S\cdot F_T = 1/T^2$ 与哈密顿量无关，从而导出一个普适的不确定关系 $Δ^2 S\,Δ^2 T \geq T^2/n^2$，其中所有系统相关的量——如热容、哈密顿量以及自由度数目——均完全抵消。这是 $S$ 与 $T$ 之间勒让德共轭性的度量学表达。我们确认能量测量是熵估计的最优方案，分析了临界点标度行为下 $F_S \sim |t|^α\to 0$ 的特性，并将 $F_S$ 与熵坐标下的鲁佩纳度规联系起来。该不确定关系被证明对所有标准热力学共轭对均成立，并探讨了冯·诺依曼熵在雷尼熵族中的特殊地位。最后，我们将结论推广至巨正则系综与广义吉布斯系综。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We derive the quantum Fisher information for entropy estimation in a Gibbs state and show that $F_s = 1/C_v$, dual to the temperature Fisher information $F_S = C_v/T^2$. Their product $F_S\cdot F_T = 1/T^2$ is independent of the Hamiltonian, yielding the universal uncertainty relation $Δ^2 S\,Δ^2 T \geq T^2/n^2$ in which all system-specific quantities such as heat capacity, the Hamiltonian, and the number of degrees of freedom cancel identically. This is the metrological expression of the Legendre conjugacy between $S$ and $T$. We identify energy measurement as the optimal protocol for entropy estimation, analyse critical-point scaling where $F_S \sim |t|^α\to 0$, and connect $F_S$ to the Ruppeiner metric in entropy coordinates. The uncertainty relation is shown to hold for all standard thermodynamic conjugate pairs, and we examine the distinguished role of the von~Neumann entropy within the Rényi family. Generalisations to the grand canonical and generalised Gibbs ensembles are given.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: Gibbs state, quantum Fisher information, entropy estimation, uncertainty relation, thermodynamic conjugate pairs, Ruppeiner metric, von Neumann entropy, critical-point scaling

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了使用量子参数估计技术通过被动线性光学方法估计表面粗糙度的极限精度，并证明了一种基于空间模式解复用的量子启发成像技术对于估计轴向标准偏差是最优的。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 表面粗糙度是众多工程与精密制造领域的重要参数。本文研究了通过被动线性光学方法估算样本均方根粗糙度的问题。借助量子参数估计技术，我们确定了粗糙度估计的最终精度极限。特别地，我们证明了多个非相干点源的轴向轮廓分布的一阶矩（平均高度）与标准差（粗糙度）信息受限于一个常数。虽然经典成像技术无法达到该极限，但一种基于空间模式解复用的量子启发成像技术被证明在估计轴向标准差方面是最优的。结合近期研究的类似径向轮廓估计方法，这可为突破衍射极限测量近光滑表面区域的粗糙度提供一种强有力的技术手段。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Surface roughness is an important quantity to many engineering and precision manufacturing disciplines. In this paper we investigate the problem of estimating the root-mean-square roughness of a sample by passive linear optical methods. By adopting quantum parameter estimation techniques, we determine the ultimate precision limits on roughness estimation. In particular, we show that the information on the first moment (mean height) and standard deviation (roughness) of the axial profile distribution of multiple incoherent point sources is bounded by a constant. While classical imaging techniques fail to achieve this bound, a quantum inspired imaging technique based on spatial mode demultiplexing is proven to be optimal for estimating the axial standard deviation. Combined with analogous recently investigated methods for estimating radial profiles, this can provide a powerful technique for measuring roughness of nearly smooth surface patches beyond the diffraction limit.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum parameter estimation, surface roughness, optical measurement, precision limits, spatial mode demultiplexing, root-mean-square roughness, axial profile distribution, diffraction limit

### 225. ❌ Bridging Classical Sensitivity and Quantum Scrambling: A Tutorial on Out-of-Time-Ordered Correlators

**作者**: Stephen Wiggins
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17

**评分理由**: 论文研究量子混沌与经典动力学的数学联系，特别是通过OTOC（out-of-time-ordered correlator）探讨量子力学中的算子非对易性与经典混沌敏感性之间的关系，属于理论物理、量子信息和应用数学领域。所有评分关键词均涉及医学影像分析、AI医疗应用等临床医学技术，与论文的量子物理主题完全无关，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该教程通过详细阐述OTOC的数学机制，探讨了经典混沌敏感性如何转化为量子力学中的算子非对易性，并区分了局部不稳定性和全局混沌，为理解经典与量子动力学提供了统一的理论框架。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 在经典动力系统中，混沌行为通常与初始条件的指数敏感性及全局相空间结构相关联。将这一几何概念转换到量子力学严格的线性框架中，构成了一个概念上的难题。无序时序关联函数（out-of-time-ordered correlator，OTOC）常被视作经典蝴蝶效应的量子类比，但这一通俗表述可能掩盖重要的数学差异。本教程通过详细阐述OTOC的数学机制，弥合了应用数学与量子信息学之间的鸿沟。我们探讨了经典敏感性如何转化为算符的非对易性，为何标准的两点关联函数无法清晰探测这种敏感性，以及量子可观测量离域化如何与经典的混合概念相联系。关键的是，我们界定了OTOC能够与无法诊断的内容，区分了局部不稳定性与全局混沌。最终，我们提供了一幅精确且可用的概念图景，探讨了库普曼-冯·诺伊曼形式体系如何为通过共享的线性视角审视经典与量子动力学提供框架。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> In classical dynamical systems, chaotic behavior is often associated with exponential sensitivity to initial conditions together with global phase-space structure. Translating this geometric concept to the strictly linear framework of quantum mechanics presents a conceptual puzzle. The out-of-time-ordered correlator (OTOC) is often motivated as the quantum analogue of the classical butterfly effect, but this slogan can hide important mathematical distinctions. This tutorial bridges the gap between applied mathematics and quantum information by detailing the mathematical machinery of the OTOC. We explore how classical sensitivity translates to operator non-commutativity, why standard two-point correlation functions fail to cleanly detect this sensitivity, and how the delocalization of quantum observables relates to classical notions of mixing. Crucially, we outline what the OTOC can and cannot diagnose, distinguishing between local instability and global chaos. Ultimately, we provide a precise and usable conceptual map, exploring how the Koopman-von Neumann formalism offers a framework to view classical and quantum dynamics through a shared linear perspective.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: out-of-time-ordered correlator, quantum chaos, classical dynamical systems, operator non-commutativity, Koopman-von Neumann formalism, quantum scrambling, butterfly effect, quantum information

### 226. ❌ Chipmunq: Fault-Tolerant Compiler for Chiplet Quantum Architectures

**作者**: Peter Wegmann, Aleksandra Świerkowska, Emmanouil Giortamis, Pramod Bhatotia
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17

**评分理由**: 论文《Chipmunq: Fault-Tolerant Compiler for Chiplet Quantum Architectures》专注于量子计算领域，具体研究容错量子电路的编译器和芯片架构映射问题。论文内容涉及量子错误校正、芯片架构、编译器设计、电路映射和路由等，与给定的所有医学影像分析、深度学习医疗影像、AI诊断、预后预测、手术规划、多模态医疗影像、医疗影像基础模型等关键词完全无关。所有关键词均得0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文解决了容错量子电路在模块化芯片架构上的编译和映射问题，提出的Chipmunq编译器显著提升了编译速度、减少了电路深度和SWAP门数量，并改善了逻辑错误率。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 随着量子计算通过量子纠错向容错方向演进，模块化芯粒架构应运而生，它能够在突破单片芯片制造极限的同时，提供所需的大规模量子比特数量。然而，这一转变引发了一个关键的编译鸿沟：现有框架无法在管理芯粒后端噪声大、连接稀疏特性的同时，处理容错量子电路的规模。
> 
> 我们提出Chipmunq，这是首个面向硬件、能将容错量子电路映射并路由至模块化架构的编译器。Chipmunq采用一种量子纠错感知的分区策略，该策略能保持逻辑量子比特补丁的完整性，从而避免了通用编译器中常见的、代价高昂的门开销。我们的评估表明，与最先进工具相比，Chipmunq的编译时间实现了13.5倍的加速。通过纳入芯粒约束和有缺陷量子比特，它在不同编码距离下将电路深度降低了86.4%，SWAP门数量减少了91.4%。至关重要的是，Chipmunq克服了芯粒间异构连接的挑战，将逻辑错误率提升高达两个数量级。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> As quantum computing advances toward fault-tolerance through quantum error correction, modular chiplet architectures have emerged to provide the massive qubit counts required while overcoming fabrication limits of monolithic chips. However, this transition introduces a critical compilation gap: existing frameworks cannot handle the scale of fault-tolerant quantum circuits while managing the noisy, sparse interconnects of chiplet backends.
>   We present Chipmunq, the first hardware-aware compiler for mapping and routing fault-tolerant circuits onto modular architectures. Chipmunq employs a quantum-error-correction-aware partitioning strategy that preserves the integrity of logical qubit patches, preventing prohibitive gate overheads common in general-purpose compilers. Our evaluation demonstrates that Chipmunq achieves a 13.5x speedup in compilation time compared to state-of-the-art tools. By incorporating chiplet constraints and defective qubits, it reduces circuit depth by 86.4% and SWAP gate counts by 91.4% across varying code distances. Crucially, Chipmunq overcomes heterogeneous inter-chiplet links, improving logical error rates by up to two orders of magnitude.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum computing, fault-tolerant compiler, chiplet architectures, quantum error correction, circuit mapping, hardware-aware compilation, logical qubit patches, inter-chiplet links

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文通过引入反事实因果中介框架，分析量子机器学习中性能提升的来源，发现当前变分量子电路的直接架构贡献远超过量子介导效应，表明其量子潜力未充分发挥。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 将量子机器学习中的性能提升归因于真正的量子资源而非经典架构扩展，仍是一个开放的方法论挑战。我们通过引入反事实因果中介框架来解决这一问题，该框架将不同架构间的性能差异分解为直接效应（源于电路参数化与表达能力）和由量子信息论可观测量中介的间接效应：纠缠熵、纯度、线性熵及量子互信息。将此框架应用于五种电路拓扑和三个基准数据集（涵盖43个已验证配置）表明，架构的直接贡献系统性超过量子中介效应，平均比值为13.1:1，平均间接贡献仅为0.82%。这些结果表明，当前变分量子电路（variational quantum circuits）的运行水平远低于其量子潜力，而基于原理的资源感知电路设计是实现可测量的量子中介性能提升的有效路径。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Attributing performance gains in quantum machine learning to genuine quantum resources rather than to classical architectural scaling remains an open methodological challenge. We address this by introducing a counterfactual causal mediation framework that decomposes inter-architectural performance differences into direct effects, attributable to circuit parameterization and expressivity, and indirect effects mediated by quantum information-theoretic observables: entanglement entropy, purity, linear entropy, and quantum mutual information. Applying this framework to five circuit topologies and three benchmark datasets (across 43 validated configurations) reveals that direct architectural contributions systematically exceed quantum-mediated effects, with a mean ratio of 13.1:1 and a mean indirect contribution of 0.82%. These results suggest that current variational quantum circuits operate substantially below their quantum potential, and that principled resource-aware circuit design represents a tractable path toward measurable quantum-mediated performance gains.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum machine learning, quantum circuits, causal mediation framework, quantum information theory, entanglement entropy, variational quantum circuits, performance attribution, quantum resource analysis
