!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了量子计算模型下广义退化字符串的模式匹配问题，将经典算法的O(mn+N)时间复杂度改进为量子算法的Õ(√(mnN))时间复杂度。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 退化字符串是一种由字符集合构成的序列。广义退化字符串将这一概念扩展为由字符串集合构成的序列，其中同一集合内的字符串具有相同长度。在广义退化字符串中寻找模式串的精确匹配可在$O(mn+N)$时间内完成（Ascone等人，WABI 2024），其中$m$为模式串长度，$n$为字符串数量，$N$为构成广义退化字符串的字符串总长度。我们改进该算法以适用于量子计算模型，实现了$\tilde{O}(\sqrt{mnN})$的运行时间。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> A degenerate string is a sequence of sets of characters. A generalized degenerate (GD) string extends this notion to the sequence of sets of strings, where strings of the same set are of equal length. Finding an exact match for a pattern string inside a GD string can be done in $O(mn+N)$ time (Ascone et al., WABI 2024), where $m$ is the pattern length, $n$ is the number of strings and $N$ the total length of strings constituting the GD string. We modify this algorithm to work under a quantum model of computation, achieving running time $\tilde{O}(\sqrt{mnN})$.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum computing, pattern matching, degenerate strings, generalized degenerate strings, quantum algorithms, string algorithms, computational complexity, quantum model of computation

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究通过引入磁振子自由度到光力学系统中，构建了光子-声子-磁振子耦合系统，实现了与机械旋转相关的可调谐慢光到快光转换，克服了传统光力学系统调谐性受限的问题。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 腔光力学已实现慢光至快光的转换，但传统光力学系统因机械频率固定而存在可调谐性受限的问题。为突破这一限制，我们在光力学系统中引入磁振子自由度，构建了集成光子、声子与磁振子的复合系统。我们建立了光磁-拉盖尔-高斯旋转系统的理论模型，并对法诺共振与群延迟进行了数值模拟。通过调控磁振子自由度，我们不仅实现了与磁振子相关的慢光至快光转换，还成功实现了与机械旋转相关的此类转换效应——这一成果有效克服了纯光力学系统固有的可调谐性局限，拓展了光转换效应的频率覆盖范围。值得注意的是，我们通过连续控制场频率调制以调节腔模失谐，数值演示了双向光速转换（慢光至快光与快光至慢光）。此外，研究结果表明调节光磁参数可在多个频率实现慢光与快光之间的动态切换。本工作为多频段光速调控提供了一个灵活平台，在全光网络与量子通信领域具有潜在应用价值。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Cavity optomechanics has enabled slow-to-fast light conversion, but traditional optomechanic systems suffer from limited tunability due to fixed mechanical frequencies. To address this constraint, we introduce a magnon degree of freedom into an optomechanical system, constructing a system that integrates photons, phonons, and magnons. We establish the theoretical model of the optomagnonic-Laguerre-Gaussian rotational system, and present numerical simulations of Fano resonances and group delay. By manipulating the magnon degree of freedom, we not only achieve slow-to-fast light conversion associated with magnons but also successfully realize such conversion effects associated with mechanical rotation-this achievement effectively overcomes the inherent tunability limitations of pure optomechanical systems and expands the frequency coverage of light conversion effects. Notably, we numerically demonstrate bidirectional light speed conversion (slow-to-fast and fast-to-slow) via continuous control field frequency modulation to tune cavity mode detuning. Additionally, our results show that adjusting optomagnonic parameters enables dynamic switching between slow light and fast light at multiple frequencies. This work provides a flexible platform for multi-frequency light speed control, with potential applications in all-optical networks and quantum communications.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: optomagnonic coupling, slow-to-fast light conversion, Laguerre-Gaussian rotational system, Fano resonance, group delay, cavity optomechanics, magnon degree of freedom, all-optical networks

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们直接观测了由自发参量下转换（SPDC）产生的X射线光子对的远场关联。通过使用能量分辨的二维光子计数探测器，我们记录了宽带宽范围内两个光子的完整环形发射，并直接从原始事件中提取光子对关联，无需施加角度约束。环形半径随光子能量变化而缩放，这与横向相位匹配条件在定量上完全一致，从而为X射线SPDC提供了严格的动量空间验证。这些观测结果为利用X射线成像与计量学中的量子关联开辟了新途径，包括关联增强的放大效应和降低模糊度。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We directly observe far-field correlations of x-ray photon pairs generated by spontaneous parametric down-conversion (SPDC). Using an energy-resolved, two-dimensional photon counting detector we record the full ring-shaped emission of both photons across a broad bandwidth and extract pair correlations directly from raw events without imposing angular constraints. The ring radii scale with photon energy, in quantitative agreement with transverse phase matching, providing a stringent momentum-space validation of x-ray SPDC. These observations open a route to leveraging quantum correlations in x-ray imaging and metrology, including correlation-enhanced magnification and reduced blurring.

</details>

### 231. ❌ Quantum Brownian Motion: proving that the Schmid transition belongs to the Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless universality class

**作者**: Francesco G. Capone, Antonio de Candia, Vittorio Cataudella, Rosario Fazio, Naoto Nagaosa, Carmine Antonio Perroni, Giulio De Filippis
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16227v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16227v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical image segmentation | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| AI for diagnosis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究量子布朗运动在周期势中的平衡性质，属于凝聚态物理和量子统计力学领域，涉及量子相变、蒙特卡洛模拟和路径积分形式。所有评分关键词均与医学影像分析、人工智能临床决策支持相关，而论文完全不涉及医学、影像、诊断、手术或医疗AI，因此所有关键词相关度均为0。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了量子布朗粒子在周期势中的耗散驱动施密特相变，通过世界线蒙特卡洛模拟证明该相变属于Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless普适类，并发现临界行为严格由环境谱函数的低频形式决定。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 本研究探讨了在周期势场中运动的量子布朗粒子的平衡性质，重点分析了欧姆耗散区中由耗散驱动的施密德相变的本质。通过采用路径积分表述下的世界线蒙特卡洛方法，并引入一个特定的二元序参量，我们证明了该相变属于别列津斯基-科斯特利茨-索利斯普适类。这一分类通过有限尺寸标度分析得到证实，该分析揭示了在临界点处序参量关联函数特有的对数衰减行为。该量子相变表现出极端的脆弱性：在超欧姆和亚欧姆耗散区中均会消失。关键的是，我们发现周期势的存在并未改变亚欧姆和超欧姆区中的局域化特性，在这些区域系统表现出与自由量子布朗粒子相同的定性行为。这些发现强调，临界行为的出现严格受环境谱函数低频形式的支配，该形式决定了耗散核的长程时间衰减特性。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We investigate the equilibrium properties of a quantum Brownian particle moving in a periodic potential, specifically addressing the nature of the dissipation-driven Schmid transition in the Ohmic regime. By employing World-Line Monte Carlo in the path-integral formalism and introducing a specific binary order parameter, we demonstrate that the transition belongs to the Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless universality class. This classification is substantiated through finite-size scaling analysis that reveals the characteristic logarithmic decay of the correlation functions associated with the order parameter at the critical point. Quantum phase transition turns out to be extremely fragile: it disappears in both over- and sub-Ohmic dissipation regimes. Crucially, we find that the presence of the periodic potential does not alter the localization properties in the sub-Ohmic and super-Ohmic regimes, where the system exhibits the same qualitative behavior as the free quantum Brownian particle. These findings highlight that the emergence of critical behavior is strictly governed by the low-frequency form of the environmental spectral function, which determines the long-range temporal decay of the dissipative kernel.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum Brownian motion, Schmid transition, Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless universality class, World-Line Monte Carlo, path-integral formalism, quantum phase transition, dissipative kernel, finite-size scaling analysis

### 232. ❌ An Energetic Constraint for Qubit-Qubit Entanglement

**作者**: Kiarn T. Laverick, Samyak P. Prasad, Pascale Senellart, Maria Maffei, Alexia Auffèves
**期刊/来源**: arxiv

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

|------|------|------|------|

**评分理由**: 论文研究量子比特纠缠的能量约束，属于量子物理和量子信息领域，与医学图像分析、人工智能临床决策支持等关键词完全无关。论文未涉及任何医学图像、深度学习、疾病诊断、手术规划或多模态医学数据内容。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文从能量角度分析量子比特纠缠，揭示了量子相干性与纠缠之间的能量权衡，并提出了在能量约束下优化和保障纠缠生成与分布的新指标。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们从能量视角分析量子比特间的纠缠，并揭示了量子相干性与纠缠之间的能量权衡关系。我们将每个量子比特的内能分解为相干分量与非相干分量。若量子比特对处于纯态且可分离态，则其相干能量达到最大值。在局域能量守恒过程中，随着量子比特间纠缠的建立，相干能量逐渐降低。这产生了一种“相干能量亏缺”，我们证明该亏缺等于一种公认的纠缠度量指标——负度平方。一般而言，量子比特对的状态总可表示为纯态的混合。此时，相干能量亏缺可进一步分解为量子分量和经典分量：量子分量对应各纯态的平均负度平方，经典分量则反映联合态的混合程度。通过对所有可能的纯态分解方式最小化量子亏缺，即可得到混合态的负度平方。我们的研究提出了在能量约束条件下优化和保障纠缠生成与分发的新效能指标。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We analyze qubit-qubit entanglement from an energetic perspective and reveal an energetic trade-off between quantum coherence and entanglement. We decompose each qubit internal energy into a coherent and an incoherent component. The qubits' coherent energies are maximal if the qubit-qubit state is pure and separable. They decrease as qubit-qubit entanglement builds up under locally-energy-preserving processes. This yields a "coherent energy deficit" that we show is equal to a well-known measure of entanglement, the square negativity. In general, a qubit-qubit state can always be represented as a mixture of pure states. Then, the coherent energy deficit splits into a quantum component, corresponding to the average square negativity of the pure states, and a classical one reflecting the mixedness of the joint state. Minimizing the quantum deficit over the possible pure state decompositions yields the square negativity of the mixture. Our findings bring out new figures of merit to optimize and secure entanglement generation and distribution under energetic constraints.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: qubit-qubit entanglement, energetic constraint, coherent energy deficit, square negativity, quantum coherence, entanglement generation, quantum information, quantum physics

---

### 233. ❌ Towards End-to-End Quantum Estimation of Non-Hermitian Pseudospectra

**作者**: Gengzhi Yang, Jiaqi Leng, Xiaodi Wu, Lin Lin
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是量子计算中非厄米算子的伪谱估计问题，属于量子信息、计算复杂性和量子算法领域。论文内容完全不涉及医学图像分析、深度学习、疾病诊断、手术规划或任何医疗应用。所有关键词都与医学图像分析和临床决策支持相关，而该论文专注于量子计算的理论和实验实现，因此所有关键词的相关度均为0。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了非厄米多体系统中伪谱成员判定的计算复杂性（PSPACE-hard和QMA-complete），并提出了一种结合量子奇异值变换和耗散态制备的端到端量子算法框架，并在离子阱量子计算机上进行了实验验证。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 非厄米多体系统可能存在谱不稳定性，微小的扰动可能导致本征值的显著偏移。伪谱能够量化这种不稳定性，并提供一种扰动鲁棒的诊断工具。对于逆多项式小量$ε$，我们证明：对于5-局域算符，判定点$z\in\mathbb{C}$是否$ε$-接近谱是PSPACE难问题；而对于4-局域算符，判定$z$是否位于$ε$-伪谱内是QMA完全问题。这确立了伪谱隶属度判定作为一个自然的计算目标。随后，我们提出一个具体的端到端量子计算框架用于判定伪谱隶属度，该框架结合了奇异值估计步骤与耗散态制备算法。我们提出的量子奇异值高斯滤波搜索（QSIGS）将量子奇异值变换（QSVT）与经典后处理相结合，实现了奇异值估计的海森堡极限查询复杂度。为制备合适的输入态，我们针对近似基态右奇异向量设计了一种算法性Lindbladian协议，并证明了其在Hatano–Nelson模型中的有效性。最后，我们在囚禁离子量子计算机上演示了完整流程，在一个最小非厄米量子比特模型的异常点附近，成功区分了目标伪谱内部与外部的点。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Non-Hermitian many-body systems can be spectrally unstable, so small perturbations may induce large eigenvalue shifts. The pseudospectrum quantifies this instability and provides a perturbation-robust diagnostic. For inverse-polynomially small $ε$, we show that deciding whether a point $z\in\mathbb{C}$ is $ε$-close to the spectrum is PSPACE-hard for $5$-local operators, whereas deciding whether $z$ lies in the $ε$-pseudospectrum is QMA-complete for $4$-local operators. This identifies pseudospectrum membership as a natural computational target. We then present a concrete end-to-end quantum framework for deciding pseudospectrum membership, which combines a singular-value estimation step with a dissipative state preparation algorithm. Our Quantum Singular-value Gaussian-filtered Search (QSIGS) combines quantum singular value transformation (QSVT) with classical post-processing to achieve Heisenberg-limited query scaling for singular-value estimation. To prepare suitable input states, we introduce an algorithmic Lindbladian protocol for approximate ground right singular vectors and prove its effectiveness for the Hatano--Nelson model. Finally, we demonstrate the full pipeline on a trapped-ion quantum computer and distinguish points inside and outside the target pseudospectrum near the exceptional point of a minimal non-Hermitian qubit model.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: non-Hermitian pseudospectra, quantum computation, QMA-complete, quantum singular value transformation, Lindbladian, trapped-ion quantum computer, exceptional point

### 234. ❌ A Scalable Open-Source QEC System with Sub-Microsecond Decoding-Feedback Latency

**作者**: Junyi Liu, Yi Lee, Yilun Xu, Gang Huang, Xiaodi Wu
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17

**评分理由**: 论文研究量子计算中的量子纠错系统，包括硬件架构、实时控制、低延迟解码等，所有关键词均涉及医学影像分析、疾病诊断、手术规划等医疗AI领域，与论文内容完全无关。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种开源、可扩展的量子纠错系统，实现了亚微秒级的解码反馈延迟，为大规模容错量子计算提供了完整的硬件平台。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 量子纠错（Quantum Error Correction, QEC）是实现大规模容错量子计算的关键，但其实际实施仍是一项重大的工程挑战。具体而言，QEC 需要对大量量子比特进行精确的实时控制，并对错误症状（error syndrome）进行低延迟、高吞吐量且准确的解码。尽管先前的研究大多集中于解码器设计，但任何 QEC 系统的整体性能都关键取决于其所有子系统——包括控制、通信和解码——以及它们之间的集成。
> 
> 为应对这一挑战，我们提出了一种基于 RISC-Q（一种基于 RISC-V 的量子控制架构生成器）构建的开源、全集成 QEC 系统。该系统原型在 RFSoC FPGA 上实现，集成了实时量子比特控制、可扩展的分布式多板卡架构，以及一个低延迟、高吞吐量解码流水线中的先进硬件 QEC 解码器，从而形成了一个完整的硬件平台，可直接部署用于超导量子比特。
> 
> 基于 AMD ZCU216 RFSoC 的三板卡原型实验评估表明，针对距离为 3 的表面码，其端到端 QEC 解码-反馈延迟为 446 纳秒，这包括症状汇总、网络通信、症状解码和错误分配。根据测得的子系统性能和先进解码器基准进行外推，当扩展至更大的硬件配置时，该架构能够实现直至距离为 21 的表面码（约 881 个物理量子比特）的亚微秒级解码-反馈延迟。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Quantum error correction (QEC) is essential for realizing large-scale, fault-tolerant quantum computation, yet its practical implementation remains a major engineering challenge. In particular, QEC demands precise real-time control of a large number of qubits and low-latency, high-throughput and accurate decoding of error syndromes. While most prior work has focused primarily on decoder design, the overall performance of any QEC system depends critically on all its subsystems including control, communication, and decoding, as well as their integration.
>   To address this challenge, we present an open-source, fully integrated QEC system built on RISC-Q, a generator for RISC-V-based quantum control architectures. Implemented on RFSoC FPGAs, our system prototype integrates real-time qubit control, a scalable distributed multi-board architecture, and the state-of-the-art hardware QEC decoder within a low-latency, high-throughput decoding pipeline, forming a complete hardware platform ready for deployment with superconducting qubits.
>   Experimental evaluation on a three-board prototype based on AMD ZCU216 RFSoCs demonstrates an end-to-end QEC decoding-feedback latency of 446 ns for a distance-3 surface code, including syndrome aggregation, network communication, syndrome decoding, and error distribution. Extrapolating from measured subsystem performance and state-of-the-art decoder benchmarks, the architecture can achieve sub-microsecond decoding-feedback latency up to a distance-21 surface code ($\sim$881 physical qubits) when scaled to larger hardware configurations.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum error correction, QEC system, low-latency decoding, hardware decoder, surface code, RISC-V quantum control, RFSoC FPGA, scalable architecture

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文预测了在玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体实现的模拟线性膨胀宇宙中存在时间Efimov效应，表现为声子产生的幂律增长和对数周期振荡，这些动力学可直接映射到宇宙学模式。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 埃菲莫夫效应源于标度不变性，这一基本对称性具有普适性意义。虽然空间埃菲莫夫物理已得到广泛研究，但其时间对应物的实现仍具挑战性，因为这需要一个破坏时间平移对称性、同时保留关键时间标度对称性的动力学系统。模拟宇宙学为解决这一挑战提供了强大平台，它连接了埃菲莫夫物理与宇宙学领域。本文预测，在准二维玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体中实现的模拟线性膨胀宇宙里会出现时间埃菲莫夫效应。声子模方程在时间重标度下的不变性导致了具有两种独特动力学的粒子产生：幂律增长与对数周期振荡，其中后者是埃菲莫夫效应的标志性特征。此外，这些动力学直接对应于亚视界与超视界宇宙学模式。我们的预测可通过现有实验中对密度涨落谱$S_{k}(t)$的时间平均测量直接验证。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Efimov effects arise from scale invariance, a fundamental symmetry with universal implications. While spatial Efimov physics has been extensively studied, realizing its temporal counterpart remains challenging, as it requires a dynamical system that breaks time-translation symmetry yet preserves the essential time-scaling symmetry. Analog cosmology offers a powerful platform to address this challenge, bridging the domains of Efimov physics and cosmology. Here, we predict a temporal Efimov effect in an analog linearly expanding universe realized with a quasi-two-dimensional Bose-Einstein condensate. The invariance of phonon mode equations under time rescaling leads to particle production with two distinct dynamics: power-law growth and log-periodic oscillations, with the latter being the hallmark signature of the Efimov effect. Furthermore, these dynamics map directly onto sub- and super-horizon cosmological modes. Our predictions can be directly verified through time-averaged measurements of the density-fluctuation spectrum $S_{k}(t)$ in current experiments.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: Efimov effect, analog cosmology, Bose-Einstein condensate, phonon production, time-scaling symmetry, cosmological modes, density-fluctuation spectrum

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们理论提出了一种利用克尔非线性在腔-磁子系统中实现$n$腔-磁子极化激元阻塞的方案。腔-磁子极化激元是由腔光子与磁子强耦合形成的混合准粒子。克尔非线性在极化激元能谱中引入了非谐性，从而实现了阻塞效应。我们证明，当外驱动频率与跃迁至第$n$个极化激元激发态共振时，可实现完美的$n$极化激元阻塞。此外，增加驱动强度可在保持高纯度的同时增强高阶阻塞效应。我们的工作开创了腔-磁子极化激元阻塞的研究领域，为制备可控量子资源开辟了新途径，并在量子通信与量子信息处理领域具有重要的应用潜力。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We theoretically propose a scheme to realize a $n$-cavity-magnon polariton blockade in a cavity-magnon system by utilizing the Kerr nonlinearity. Cavity-magnon polaritons are hybrid quasiparticles formed by the strong coupling between cavity photons and magnons. The Kerr nonlinearity introduces anharmonicity into the polariton energy spectrum, which in turn enables the blockade effect. We demonstrate that when the external driving frequency is resonant with the transition to the $n$th polariton excited state, a perfect $n$-polariton blockade is achieved. Moreover, increasing the driving strength enhances higher-order blockade while maintaining high purity. Our work pioneers the field of cavity-magnon polariton blockade, opens a new avenue for the preparation of controllable quantum resources and holds significant potential for applications in the fields of quantum communication and quantum information processing.

</details>
<br>

### 237. ❌ Geometric phase for an accelerated two-level atom in AdS spacetime

**作者**: Linghui Qiu, Jialin Zhang, Hongwei Yu
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16084v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16084v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<summary>评分详情</summary>

| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是理论物理中加速原子在Anti-de Sitter时空中的几何相位，属于量子场论和广义相对论交叉领域。所有评分关键词均涉及医学影像分析和人工智能在临床决策中的应用，与论文的物理理论研究内容完全无关。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了在Anti-de Sitter时空中均匀加速的两能级原子与无质量共形标量场真空涨落耦合时获得的几何相位，发现亚临界和超临界加速度下相位行为存在显著差异，且超临界情况下相位修正表现出明显的边界条件依赖性。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们研究了在反德西特（Anti-de Sitter，AdS）时空中，一个均匀加速的二能级原子与无质量共形标量场的真空涨落耦合时所获得的几何相位。利用开放量子系统形式体系，我们计算了在AdS边界上对场施加三种边界条件（狄利克雷、透明和诺伊曼）下的相位。研究结果揭示了亚临界加速与超临界加速之间的显著差异。对于亚临界加速，原子演化近似于孤立系统，其几何相位既不依赖于AdS半径，也不依赖于加速度。然而，在超临界加速情况下，拓扑-加速度诱导的相位修正会出现，并表现出明显的边界条件依赖性。当AdS半径小于原子的固有波长时，大加速度下修正量的大小遵循诺伊曼$>$透明$>$狄利克雷的排序。此外，在原子权重参数的有限区间内，狄利克雷和诺伊曼边界条件在相位修正中产生的峰结构比透明条件更为丰富，其具体模式由加速度与原子能隙之间的竞争所决定。最后，在超临界区域内的透明边界条件下，AdS相位修正与其在德西特（de Sitter，dS）时空中的对应结果高度相似。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We have investigated the geometric phase acquired by a uniformly accelerated two-level atom coupled to vacuum fluctuations of a massless conformal scalar field in Anti-de Sitter (AdS) spacetime. Using the open-quantum-system formalism, we calculate the phase under three boundary conditions (Dirichlet, transparent and Neumann) imposed on the field at the AdS boundary. Our findings reveal a sharp distinction between subcritical and supercritical accelerations. For subcritical accelerations, the atom evolves effectively as an isolated system, and the geometric phase is independent of both the AdS radius and the acceleration. For supercritical accelerations, however, topology-acceleration-induced phase corrections emerge and display pronounced boundary-condition dependence. When the AdS radius is smaller than the atomic proper wavelength, the magnitude of the correction at large accelerations follows the ordering Neumann$>$transparent$>$Dirichlet. Moreover, over a finite interval of the atomic weight parameter, both Dirichlet and Neumann boundary conditions produce a richer peak structure in the phase correction than the transparent case, with the detailed pattern governed by the competition between the acceleration and the atomic energy gap. Finally, for transparent boundary conditions in the supercritical regime, the AdS phase correction closely resembles its de Sitter (dS) counterpart.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: geometric phase, accelerated two-level atom, Anti-de Sitter spacetime, vacuum fluctuations, boundary conditions, open quantum system, phase correction, subcritical and supercritical accelerations

### 238. ❌ Population Annealing as a Discrete-Time Schrödinger Bridge

**作者**: Masayuki Ohzeki
**期刊/来源**: arxiv

<details>

| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文标题为《Population Annealing as a Discrete-Time Schrödinger Bridge》，作者为Masayuki Ohzeki。摘要内容聚焦于理论框架，将群体退火（Population Annealing）重新解释为离散时间薛定谔桥（Schrödinger Bridge）问题，并探讨了热力学最优性、最优传输几何框架、Jarzynski等式等理论概念。全文未提及任何医学图像分析、深度学习、疾病诊断、手术规划或医疗数据融合等医疗相关主题。所有评分关键词均与医学图像分析和临床决策支持相关，而该论文属于理论物理、统计力学和优化算法领域，与医疗领域完全无关。

</details>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出一个理论框架，将群体退火重新解释为离散时间薛定谔桥问题，证明了其热力学最优性，并统一了非平衡热力学与最优传输的几何框架。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们提出一个理论框架，通过离散时间薛定谇桥问题的视角重新诠释群体退火算法。我们证明，PA中的启发式重加权步骤可通过瞬时投影解析求解薛定谇系统而无需迭代计算。此外，我们识别出热力学功作为解决路径空间全局变分问题的最优控制势。这一视角将非平衡热力学与最优传输的几何框架相统一，将贾金斯基等式解释为唐斯克-瓦拉丹变分原理中的一致性条件，并阐明了PA的热力学最优性。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We present a theoretical framework that reinterprets Population Annealing (PA) through the lens of the discrete-time Schrödinger Bridge (SB) problem. We demonstrate that the heuristic reweighting step in PA is derived by analytically solving the Schrödinger system without iterative computation via instantaneous projection. In addition, we identify the thermodynamic work as the optimal control potential that solves the global variational problem on path space. This perspective unifies non-equilibrium thermodynamics with the geometric framework of optimal transport, interpreting the Jarzynski equality as a consistency condition within the Donsker-Varadhan variational principle, and elucidates the thermodynamic optimality of PA.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: Population Annealing, Schrödinger Bridge, optimal transport, thermodynamic work, Jarzynski equality, variational principle, non-equilibrium thermodynamics

### 239. ❌ Qudit Implementation of the Rodeo Algorithm for Quantum Spectral Filtering

**作者**: Julio Cesar Siqueira Rocha, Rodrigo Alves Dias
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16049v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16049v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究量子计算中的Rodeo算法和qudit实现，用于量子系统的谱分析和热力学表征，涉及量子电路、数值模拟和Ising模型。所有评分关键词均与医学图像分析、临床决策支持、疾病诊断/预后、手术规划等医学领域相关，而论文完全不涉及任何医学、生物学或临床相关内容，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了使用qudit实现Rodeo算法进行量子谱滤波的方法，通过数值模拟显示qutrit实现比qubit实现减少18%的波动，为多能级量子系统的谱分析和热力学表征提供了框架。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 量子多值比特（qudit）作为量子比特的多能级推广，为量子计算中的二元范式提供了自然延伸，并为提升算法性能创造了新机遇。除了直接适用于多能级量子系统的模拟外，高维辅助系统能够通过同时执行多个控制操作来提升量子算法的采样效率，从而降低电路复杂度。本研究致力于实现三个主要目标：首先，我们提出了采用通用 $d$ 能级辅助量子多值比特的 Rodeo 算法框架；其次，我们引入了“Rodeo 核”的概念，其定义为双频率干涉仪，在能量域中充当谱滤波器；最后，我们为 Rodeo 算法提出了一种微正则协议。该协议能够通过单次能量扫描实现熵量的估计，并可自然地解释为态密度的高斯卷积。为支撑理论分析，我们使用三维、四维和五维辅助量子多值比特对相应量子电路进行了数值评估。模拟以一维伊辛模型为对象，同时考虑了自旋-$\frac{1}{2}$ 与自旋-$1$ 粒子。与量子比特实现相比，辅助量子三值比特（qutrit）实现的波动降低了 $18\%$。我们的结果表明，量子多值比特为多能级量子系统的谱分析和热力学表征提供了一个有效框架。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Qudits, the multi-level generalization of qubits, provide a natural extension of the binary paradigm in quantum computation and offer new opportunities to enhance algorithmic performance. Beyond their direct applicability to the simulation of multi-level quantum systems, higher-dimensional ancillae can improve sampling efficiency in quantum algorithms by enabling the simultaneous implementation of multiple control operations, thereby reducing circuit complexity. In this work, we pursue three main objectives. First, we present a formulation of the Rodeo algorithm employing a general $d$-level ancilla qudit. Second, we introduce the concept of the \emph{Rodeo kernel}, defined as a two-frequency interferometer, which acts as a spectral filter in the energy domain. Finally, we propose a microcanonical protocol for the Rodeo algorithm. This protocol enables the estimation of entropic quantities through a single energy sweep and admits a natural interpretation as a Gaussian convolution of the density of states. To support the theoretical analysis, we perform numerical evaluations of the corresponding quantum circuit using ancilla qudits of dimensions three, four, and five. The simulations are performed for the one-dimensional Ising model, considering both spin-$\frac{1}{2}$ and spin-$1$ particles. The ancilla qutrit implementation exhibits an $18\%$ reduction in fluctuations compared to the qubit implementation. Our results show that the qudits provide a framework for spectral analysis and thermodynamic characterization of multi-level quantum systems.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: qudit, Rodeo algorithm, quantum spectral filtering, quantum circuit, Ising model, numerical simulation, thermodynamic characterization

### 240. ❌ Monolithic Segmented 3D Ion Trap for Quantum Technology Applications

**作者**: Abhishek Menon, Michael Strauss, George Tomaras, Liam Jeanette, April X. Sheffield, Devon Valdez, Yuanheng Xie, Visal So, Henry De Luo, Midhuna Duraisamy Suganthi, Mark Dugan, Philippe Bado, Norbert M. Linke, Guido Pagano, Roman Zhuravel
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16048v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16048v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical image segmentation | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| AI for diagnosis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是用于量子技术（量子模拟、计算、计量和网络）的单片式分段3D离子阱，涉及离子阱设计、射频电压、加热率、相干时间和量子门保真度等量子物理和工程内容。所有评分关键词均与医学图像分析、人工智能临床决策支持、疾病诊断/预后、手术规划等医学领域完全无关，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文解决了在量子技术应用中实现低加热率、高光学访问和高射频电压的单片式3D离子阱的技术挑战，并展示了一种基于熔融石英的分段刀片阱，在Yb+离子中实现了低加热率、长相干时间和高保真度两量子比特门。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 单片式三维（3D）保罗离子阱将二维（2D）芯片离子阱的高精度微加工优势，与宏观保罗离子阱（通常为手工组装）所特有的深囚禁势和低加热率特性相结合。然而，对于重离子物种（如Yb$^{+}$和Ba$^{+}$），要在维持高射频（RF）电压的同时实现低运动加热率和高数值孔径（NA）的光学接入，仍然是一项重大的技术挑战。本工作中，我们提出了一种分段式、单片化的三维熔融石英刀片离子阱，其离子-电极距离为250 $μ$m，并能在高射频电压下稳定工作。我们使用Yb$^{+}$离子对该离子阱的性能进行了基准测试，结果表明：在阱轴向中心周围200 $μ$m范围内实现了轴向均匀的囚禁势；具备高多方向光学接入能力（NA高达0.7）；在接近室温、径向囚禁频率约为3 MHz的条件下，径向运动加热率低至1.1 $\pm$ 0.1 量子/秒。此外，我们观测到径向质心模式的运动拉姆齐相干时间（$T_{2}$）约为95 ms。在进行了状态制备和测量校正后，我们实现了${99.3}^{+ 0.7}_{- 1.5}$$\%$的双量子比特门保真度。这些结果表明，熔融石英单片式刀片离子阱是一个可扩展、模块化的平台，适用于重离子物种的量子模拟、量子计算、量子计量学及量子网络研究。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Monolithic three-dimensional (3D) Paul traps combine the high-precision microfabrication of two-dimensional (2D) chip traps with the deep trapping potentials and low heating rates characteristic of macroscopic Paul traps, which are typically manually assembled. However, achieving low motional heating rates and optical access with a high numerical aperture (NA) while maintaining the high radio-frequency (RF) voltages required for heavy ionic species, such as Yb$^{+}$ and Ba$^{+}$, remains a significant technical challenge. In this work, we present a segmented, monolithic 3D fused silica blade trap, featuring an ion-electrode distance of 250 $μ$m with stable operation at high RF voltages. We benchmark the performance of the trap using Yb$^{+}$ ions, demonstrating axially homogeneous trapping potentials for 200 $μ$m around the axial center of the trap, high multi-directional optical access (up to 0.7 NA), and radial motional heating rate as low as 1.1 $\pm$ 0.1 quanta/s at radial trap frequencies about 3 MHz near room temperature. Furthermore, we observe a motional Ramsey coherence time, $T_{2}$, of around 95 ms for the radial center-of-mass mode. We demonstrate a two-qubit gate fidelity of ${99.3}^{+ 0.7}_{- 1.5}$$\%$ with state preparation and measurement correction. These results establish fused-silica monolithic blade traps as a scalable, modular platform for quantum simulation, computation, metrology, and networking with heavy ionic species.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: monolithic 3D ion trap, segmented blade trap, Yb+ ions, motional heating rate, coherence time, two-qubit gate fidelity, quantum simulation, fused silica

### 241. ❌ CSS codes from the Bruhat order of Coxeter groups

**作者**: Kamil Bradler
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16036v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16036v1)

| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 该论文研究的是量子纠错码（CSS codes）的构造方法，基于Coxeter群的Bruhat偏序结构，属于纯数学和量子计算领域。论文内容完全不涉及医学图像分析、深度学习、疾病诊断、手术规划或任何医疗应用。所有关键词均与医学图像和临床决策支持相关，而本文专注于代数拓扑和量子信息理论，因此所有关键词的相关度均为0。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种基于Coxeter群Bruhat偏序结构生成具有特定参数的CSS量子纠错码的方法，并展示了如何控制稳定子权重或处理不规则权重分布。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 本文提出一种生成具有特定参数族的CSS码构造方法。研究对象为有限或无限（可约或不可约）的Coxeter群，以及一种基于几何动机、以Bruhat命名的Coxeter群元素偏序关系。已知Bruhat序与代数拓扑存在关联——它同时作为面偏序集，刻画了正则CW复形中$p$维胞腔的包含关系，这一特性使其在量子纠错码设计中具有重要意义。借助Coxeter群特有的Bruhat面偏序区间结构，本文证明对应的链复形可转化为多类CSS码。根据具体构造策略，可获得具有受控稳定子权重的CSS码（及其族），例如$[6006, 924, \{{\leq14},{\leq7}\}]$（稳定子权重为14和9）与$[22880,3432,\{{\leq8},{\leq16}\}]$（权重为16和10），以及具有高度非均匀稳定子权重分布的CSS码如$[571,199,\{5,5\}]$。针对后者，本文发展了一种权重约简方法以处理罕见的重稳定子。最后，展示了如何提取可解释为带元校验的CSS码的四项（长度为三）链复形。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> I introduce a method to generate families of CSS codes with interesting code parameters. The object of study is Coxeter groups, both finite and infinite (reducible or not), and a geometrically motivated partial order of Coxeter group elements named after Bruhat. The Bruhat order is known to provide a link to algebraic topology -- it doubles as a face poset capturing the inclusion relations of the $p$-dimensional cells of a regular CW~complex and that is what makes it interesting for QEC code design. Assisted by the Bruhat face poset interval structure unique to Coxeter groups I show that the corresponding chain complexes can be turned into multitudes of CSS codes. Depending on the approach, I obtain CSS codes (and their families) with controlled stabilizer weights, for example $[6006, 924, \{{\leq14},{\leq7}\}]$ (stabilizer weights~14 and 9) and $[22880,3432,\{{\leq8},{\leq16}\}]$ (weights 16 and 10), and CSS codes with highly irregular stabilizer weight distributions such as $[571,199,\{5,5\}]$. For the latter, I develop a weight-reduction method to deal with rare heavy stabilizers. Finally, I show how to extract four-term (length three) chain complexes that can be interpreted as CSS codes with a metacheck.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: CSS codes, Coxeter groups, Bruhat order, quantum error correction, chain complexes, stabilizer weights, face poset, algebraic topology

> This technical note provides a high-level overview of the present state of basic field electron emission (FE) theory, as suitable for use in the context of technological applications of FE theory. At present there is much theoretical confusion in FE literature, and a partial breakdown of the peer review system. Even in sensitive technological contexts, many papers have stated and used out-of-date theory that makes current-density predictions that are several hundred times less than those of modern FE theory. A primary aim of this note is to help reduce the confusion and error in future published FE literature. It is not intended as a detailed review of FE theory.

</details>

### 243. ❌ A Perfectly Distributable Quantum-Classical Algorithm for Estimating Triangular Balance in a Signed Edge Stream

**作者**: Steven Kordonowy, Bibhas Adhikari, Hannes Leipold
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17

<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种可完美分发的量子-经典混合流算法，用于高效估计符号边流中不同符号配置的三角形数量，相比纯经典方法具有多项式空间优势。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们开发了一种完全可分布式量子-经典流式算法，该算法通过处理带符号边流，在单遍边流中高效估计多种带符号构型的三角形数量。我们的方法引入了用于处理带符号边流的量子草图寄存器，并结合量子估计器中查询对调用的测量算子，同时辅以一个互补的经典估计器来统计量子过程未捕获的三角形。这种混合设计相比纯经典方法实现了多项式级空间优势，将无符号边流数据的已知结果扩展至带符号场景。我们量化了随机带符号图实例中的非平衡性，展示了经典算法与混合算法在实际中如何估计平衡度。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We develop a perfectly distributable quantum-classical streaming algorithm that processes signed edges to efficiently estimate the counts of triangles of diverse signed configurations in the single pass edge stream. Our approach introduces a quantum sketch register for processing the signed edge stream, together with measurement operators for query-pair calls in the quantum estimator, while a complementary classical estimator accounts for triangles not captured by the quantum procedure. This hybrid design yields a polynomial space advantage over purely classical approaches, extending known results from unsigned edge stream data to the signed setting. We quantify the lack of balance on random signed graph instances, showcasing how the classical and hybrid algorithms estimate balance in practice.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum-classical algorithm, signed edge stream, triangle balance estimation, distributable streaming algorithm, quantum sketch register, hybrid design, polynomial space advantage, signed graph instances

### 244. ❌ 3D tomography of exchange phase in a Si/SiGe quantum dot device

**作者**: Dylan Albrecht, Sarah Thompson, N. Tobias Jacobson, Ryan Jock

**评分理由**: 论文研究量子计算中的自旋量子比特设备，涉及3D断层扫描、相位提取和电压空间建模，属于量子物理和计算领域。所有评分关键词均针对医学影像分析和临床决策支持，与论文内容完全无关。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文解决了从自旋量子比特设备中提取交换相互作用相位的问题，通过结合相位偏移数字全息术和最大流/最小割相位展开方法，在3D电压空间中稳健地建模相位体积，以优化量子比特控制。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 交换相互作用是自旋量子处理器运行的基础构建单元。提取交换相互作用系数 $J(\mathbf{V})$（作为栅极电压的函数），对于理解无序性、精确模拟器件性能以及高保真度地操作自旋量子比特至关重要。在自旋量子比特器件中，典型的交换相干测量会得到一个累积相位的调制余弦值，而该累积相位本身又是交换作用的时间积分。因此，从实验数据中提取 $J(\mathbf{V})$ 十分困难，原因在于反演余弦函数存在多值性、相位解卷绕对噪声敏感，以及反演积分本身的问题。作为获取 $J(\mathbf{V})$ 的一个步骤，我们首先解决了前两个挑战，以揭示累积相位 $φ(\mathbf{V})$。我们融合了多个领域的技术，从一系列二维测量中稳健地提取并建模了自旋量子比特器件的三维相位体。具体而言，我们提出了一种测量技术来获取包裹相位（类似于相移数字全息术中的方法），并利用最大流/最小割相位解卷绕方法（PUMA）在三维电压空间中解卷绕相位。我们证明了该方法对器件中观测到的最小漂移具有鲁棒性，这一点通过提高扫描分辨率得到了验证。在建立提取相位的模型后，我们对模型进行优化，以在电压空间中定位一个梯度最小的 $π$ 交换脉冲点。我们的测量方案可能提供详细信息，有助于理解影响器件良率的器件变异性的根源，能够在操作期间针对特定器件校准器件模型以实现更精细的误差归因，并支持对量子比特控制进行系统性优化。我们预计，本文提出的方法可能适用于其他量子比特平台。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> The exchange interaction is a foundational building block for the operation of spin-based quantum processors. Extracting the exchange interaction coefficient $J(\mathbf{V})$, as a function of gate electrode voltages, is important for understanding disorder, faithfully simulating device performance, and operating spin qubits with high fidelity. Typical coherent measurements of exchange in spin qubit devices yield a modulated cosine of an accumulated phase, which in turn is the time integral of exchange. As such, extracting $J(\mathbf{V})$ from experimental data is difficult due to the ambiguity of inverting a cosine, the sensitivity to noise when unwrapping phase, as well as the problem of inverting the integral. As a step toward obtaining $J(\mathbf{V})$, we tackle the first two challenges to reveal the accumulated phase, $φ(\mathbf{V})$. We incorporate techniques from a wide range of fields to robustly extract and model a 3D phase volume for spin qubit devices from a sequence of 2D measurements. In particular, we present a measurement technique to obtain the wrapped phase, as done in phase-shifting digital holography, and utilize the max-flow/min-cut phase unwrapping method (PUMA) to unwrap the phase in 3D voltage space. We show this method is robust to the minimal observed drift in the device, which we confirm by increasing scan resolution. Upon building a model of the extracted phase, we optimize over the model to locate a minimal-gradient $π$ exchange pulse point in voltage space. Our measurement protocol may provide detailed information useful for understanding the origins of device variability governing device yield, enable calibrating device models to specific devices during operation for more sophisticated error attribution, and enable a systematic optimization of qubit control. We anticipate that the methods presented here may be applicable to other qubit platforms.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: spin qubit, exchange interaction, phase extraction, 3D tomography, voltage space, quantum processor, phase unwrapping, quantum control

It is well known that OQWs provide a general framework for implementing quantum computation. As a proof of principle, we demonstrate the feasibility of running this algorithm within the open quantum walk computation model, and we show that its expected runtime remains finite even in the slower regime.

### 246. ❌ Anomalous dynamical scaling in interacting anyonic chains

**作者**: Xu-Chen Yang, Botao Wang, Jianpeng Liu, Bing Yang, Jianmin Yuan, Yongqiang Li
**期刊/来源**: arxiv

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是量子物理中的任意子统计与非平衡动力学，涉及一维晶格、量子模拟、数值模拟和标度分析，完全不涉及医学图像分析、深度学习、疾病诊断、手术规划或任何医疗健康相关内容。所有关键词均与论文主题无关。

<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了任意子统计如何导致非平衡量子动力学中的反常普适标度行为，发现粒子输运与信息传播之间存在分离：密度关联超扩散传播，而纠缠熵呈弹道增长。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 粒子统计对非平衡量子动力学施加了基本约束，然而分数统计能否超越传统的玻色-费米范式引发出新的普适动力学标度行为，仍是一个开放问题。本文研究了一维晶格中任意子远离平衡的多体弛豫过程，揭示了由分数统计主导的非传统却普适的标度行为。基于大规模数值模拟与标度分析，我们发现粒子输运与信息传播之间存在明显分离：密度关联呈超扩散传播，而纠缠熵则以弹道方式增长。这种反常粒子动力学可从统计相位诱导的量子干涉角度直观理解，该干涉抑制了相干空穴-双粒子（holon-doublon）的传播。相比之下，纠缠增长则受其构型分量的主导并以弹道速度传播。我们的研究确立了任意子统计可作为超越玻色子与费米子的全新普适非平衡动力学来源，对当前量子模拟实验具有直接参考价值。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Particle statistics impose fundamental constraints on nonequilibrium quantum dynamics, yet it remains an open question whether fractional statistics can lead to emergent universal dynamical scaling beyond the conventional Bose-Fermi paradigm. Here we investigate the far-from-equilibrium many-body relaxation of anyons in a one-dimensional lattice and uncover an unconventional yet universal scaling behavior governed by fractional statistics. Based on large-scale numerical simulations and scaling analysis, we identify a distinct separation between particle transport and information spreading: density correlations spread superdiffusively, whereas entanglement entropy grows ballistically. The anomalous particle dynamics can be interpreted intuitively from the statistical-phase-induced quantum interference, which suppresses coherent holon-doublon propagation. In contrast, the entanglement growth turns out to be dominated by its configurational component, which propagates ballistically. Our results establish anyonic statistics as a distinct source of universal nonequilibrium dynamics beyond bosons and fermions, with direct relevance to current quantum simulation experiments.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: anyonic statistics, nonequilibrium quantum dynamics, universal scaling, particle transport, entanglement entropy, quantum simulation, one-dimensional lattice, fractional statistics

### 247. ❌ Simultaneous amplitude and phase spectroscopy using two-photon interference

**作者**: Kyle M. Jordan, Yingwen Zhang, Frédéric Bouchard, Duncan England, Philip J. Bustard, Benjamin J. Sussman, Jeff S. Lundeen, Andrew H. Proppe
**期刊/来源**: arxiv

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出并演示了一种使用纠缠光子对的量子光谱学方案，能够同时以极低光强和快速采集时间测量样品的吸收和相移，实现了对样品完整线性光学响应的测量。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 量子光谱学旨在利用非经典光探测化学体系，其特性在定性和定量上均不同于传统光源。一种前景广阔的技术是利用强度关联的双光束来抑制吸收光谱中固有的噪声源。然而，化学样品引起的相移测量——其可提供与吸收互补的信息——仍然是一个挑战。在此，我们提出并演示了一种利用纠缠光子对的方案，该方案能够以极低的光强和相对较快的数分钟采集时间，同时测量样品的吸收和相移。该方法将先前强度关联的应用与利用双光子干涉的宽带量子干涉仪相结合，以测量样品的完整线性光学响应。我们的研究表明，通过选择合适的探测光束和检测方案，吸收的精确测量也可具备相位敏感性。这为实现一类新型量子光谱学方案奠定了基础，该类方案可通过单次探测同时测量吸收和相位。我们的技术适用于多种化学和生物样品（如量子点和有机荧光团）的表征，并可能对受光强限制的光谱测量具有重要价值。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Quantum spectroscopy seeks to probe chemical systems using nonclassical light, which has properties that are qualitatively and quantitatively different than conventional light sources. One promising technique uses intensity-correlated twin beams of light to reduce the noise sources inherent to absorption spectroscopy. However, measurements of the phase shift imparted by the chemical sample, which provides complementary information to the absorption, continue to be a challenge. Here, we propose and demonstrate a scheme using entangled photon pairs that can simultaneously measure both the absorption and phase shift of a sample with extremely low optical intensities and with relatively fast few-minute acquisition times. This method combines the previous use of intensity correlations with a broadband quantum interferometer utilizing two-photon interference to measure the complete linear optical response of the sample. Our work shows that precise measurements of absorption can also be made phase-sensitive using suitable choices of probe beam and detection scheme. This enables a new class of quantum spectroscopy schemes which measure absorption and phase with a single probe. Our technique is relevant to the characterization of a wide array of chemical and biological samples, such as quantum dots and organic fluorophores, and may be useful for spectroscopic measurements that are otherwise constrained in intensity.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum spectroscopy, entangled photon pairs, absorption measurement, phase shift measurement, two-photon interference, intensity correlations, optical response, chemical samples

### 248. ❌ Riemannian gradient descent for Hartree-Fock theory

**作者**: Evgueni Dinvay
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-16
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15870v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15870v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical image segmentation | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| AI for diagnosis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文《Riemannian gradient descent for Hartree-Fock theory》研究的是量子化学中的电子结构优化问题，具体涉及Hartree-Fock理论的黎曼优化框架、无限维Stiefel和Grassmann流形、Sobolev空间H^1中的数值方法等。所有评分关键词均属于医学影像分析和临床决策支持领域（如医学图像分割、深度学习医学成像、AI诊断、预后预测、手术规划、多模态医学成像、医学影像基础模型），而该论文完全不涉及任何医学、生物学、临床或影像相关的内容，属于纯粹的计算数学和量子化学领域。因此，所有关键词的相关度均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一个在Sobolev空间H^1中直接表述的Hartree-Fock理论的黎曼优化框架，通过无限维Stiefel和Grassmann流形处理正交约束，并开发了黎曼最速下降法和预处理非线性共轭梯度法，数值实验表明该方法相比传统SCF-DIIS方案具有鲁棒收敛性和竞争性能。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 本文提出了一种直接在索博列夫空间$H^1$中表述的哈特里-福克理论的黎曼优化框架。正交归一性约束通过赋予嵌入$H^1$度量的无限维斯蒂费尔流形和格拉斯曼流形进行几何解释。利用预解算子导出了欧几里得梯度、黎曼梯度、切空间投影及回缩的显式表达式，避免了分布形式的表述。所得算法包括黎曼最速下降法和一种配备阿米霍回溯与鲍威尔型重启的预处理非线性共轭梯度法。特别关注了基于动能算子求逆的、具有物理动机的预处理技术。该框架天然兼容自适应多小波离散化方案，其中库仑型卷积可被高效计算。数值实验表明，与传统SCF-DIIS方案相比，本方法具有稳健的收敛性和有竞争力的性能。此外，对于小分子体系，梯度下降法能够从随机初始猜测实现收敛。所提出的框架为电子结构优化提供了一个几何一致且与离散化无关的视角，并为量子化学中无限维黎曼方法的进一步发展奠定了基础。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We present a Riemannian optimization framework for Hartree-Fock theory formulated directly in the Sobolev space $H^1$. The orthonormality constraints are interpreted geometrically via infinite-dimensional Stiefel and Grassmann manifolds endowed with the embedded $H^1$ metric. Explicit expressions for Euclidean and Riemannian gradients, tangent-space projections, and retractions are derived using resolvent operators, avoiding distributional formulations. The resulting algorithms include Riemannian steepest descent and a preconditioned nonlinear conjugate gradient method equipped with Armijo backtracking and Powell-type restarts. Particular attention is given to physically motivated preconditioning based on inversion of the kinetic energy operator. The framework is naturally compatible with adaptive multiwavelet discretizations, where Coulomb-type convolutions can be evaluated efficiently. Numerical experiments demonstrate robust convergence and competitive performance compared to conventional SCF-DIIS schemes. In addition, for small molecules the gradient descent method converges from random initial guesses. The proposed formulation provides a geometrically consistent and discretization-independent perspective on electronic structure optimization and offers a foundation for further developments in infinite-dimensional Riemannian methods for quantum chemistry.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: Riemannian optimization, Hartree-Fock theory, Sobolev space H^1, Stiefel manifold, Grassmann manifold, electronic structure optimization, quantum chemistry, preconditioned conjugate gradient

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出通过最小化局部能量的对数压缩方差来改进神经网络波函数在量子多体系统能量计算中的收敛性，并展示了该方法在二维谐振子陷阱中自旋-1/2粒子系统的有效性。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 神经网络正成为确定相互作用多体费米子系统量子态的有力工具。标准方法通过最小化基于蒙特卡洛样本估计的平均局域能量来训练神经网络拟设。然而，这通常会导致估计平均能量的样本间波动较大，从而使能量最小化的收敛速度缓慢。我们提出，最小化局域能量的对数压缩方差可以显著改善收敛性。此外，该损失函数可通过调整以在多轮运行中系统性地获取能谱。我们以二维谐振子势阱中具有相反自旋粒子间吸引性Pöschl-Teller相互作用的自旋-1/2粒子体系验证了这些构想。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Neural networks are emerging as a powerful tool for determining the quantum states of interacting many-body fermionic systems. The standard approach trains a neural-network ansatz by minimizing the mean local energy estimated from Monte Carlo samples. However, this typically results in large sample-to-sample fluctuations in the estimated mean energy and thus slow convergence of the energy minimization. We propose that minimizing a logarithmically compressed variance of the local energies can dramatically improve convergence. Moreover, this loss function can be adapted to systematically obtain the energy spectrum across multiple runs. We demonstrate these ideas for spin-1/2 particles in a 2D harmonic trap with attractive Poschl-Teller interactions between opposite spins.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: neural network wave functions, quantum many-body states, energy minimization, Monte Carlo sampling, local energy variance, fermionic systems, convergence improvement

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 可编程线性光学干涉仪是光信号处理、量子信息处理及光子计算领域的核心基础元件。现有光子集成方案采用马赫-曾德尔干涉仪网状结构实现任意$M$模式酉变换，但其占地面积与累积损耗随光学元件数量呈$O(M^2)$规模增长。本文提出并实验验证了一种基于多平面光转换（MPLC）的可编程架构，该架构可直接对空间拼接的自由空间像素模式实施线性光学变换。在此架构中，横向晶格排列的$M$个空间模式通过一系列由自由空间传播段分隔的可编程相位掩模板，经历酉变换后映射至几何结构完全相同的$M个输出模式。数值模拟表明，任意$M$模式酉变换可通过相位掩模板数量近似线性于$M$的规模编译实现目标高保真度。基于空间光调制器的MPLC系统，我们实验演示了作用于最多16个空间像素模式的可编程干涉仪，包括可调谐分束器、哈达玛酉变换、空间置换、增强型贝尔测量酉变换以及特定模式子集的部分酉变换。这些成果确立了基于MPLC的像素模式干涉仪作为一种极具前景的可编程线性光学架构，在经典与量子光学互连、光子交换及量子信息处理等领域具有重要应用价值。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Programmable linear optical interferometers are a core primitive in optical signal processing, quantum information processing, and photonic computing. Existing photonic-integrated implementations realize arbitrary $M$-mode unitaries using Mach--Zehnder-interferometer meshes whose footprint and accumulated loss scale with $O(M^2)$ optical components. Here we analyze and experimentally demonstrate a programmable architecture for implementing linear optical transformations directly on spatially tiled free-space pixel modes using multi-plane light conversion (MPLC). In this architecture, $M$ spatial modes arranged on a transverse lattice undergo a unitary transformation and are mapped to $M$ output modes of identical geometry through a sequence of programmable phase masks separated by free-space propagation segments. Numerical simulations show that arbitrary $M$-mode unitaries can be compiled to a desired high fidelity using a number of phase planes that scales approximately linearly with $M$. Using a spatial-light-modulator-based MPLC, we experimentally demonstrate programmable interferometers acting on up to $16$ spatial pixel modes, including tunable beamsplitters, Hadamard unitaries, spatial permutations, boosted-Bell-measurement unitaries, and partial unitaries on select subsets of modes. These results establish MPLC-based pixel-mode interferometers as a promising architecture for programmable linear optics with applications in classical and quantum optical interconnects, photonic switching, and quantum information processing.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: programmable linear interferometers, multi-plane light conversion, spatial pixel modes, optical signal processing, quantum information processing, photonic computing, spatial-light modulator, free-space propagation

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文解决了量子计算机上晶格规范场论模拟中无限维自由度正则化的开放问题，通过任意子正则化方法将U(1)和SU(2)规范场耦合到费米子物质，并提供了在容错量子计算机上实现该模型的量子电路构造。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 无限维自由度的最优正则化是量子计算机上晶格规范理论可处理模拟的核心开放问题。本文考虑通过将规范群$G$替换为编织融合范畴来正则化规范场，该范畴的对象对应于陈-西蒙斯理论$G_k$的威尔逊线，其中能级$k$作为正则化参数。我们展示了如何利用融合表面模型框架将这些正则化的$U(1)$和$SU(2)$规范群与费米子物质耦合，该框架将物质与规范场激发视为相互作用的任意子。随后，我们探讨了在容错量子计算机上模拟所构建哈密顿量的方法，为模型中基本门的实现提供了显式量子电路构造——即$U(1)_k$和$SU(2)_k$任意子理论中的$F$符号与$R$符号，这些构造本身可能具有独立的研究价值。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> The optimal regularization of infinite-dimensional degrees of freedom is a central open problem in the tractable simulation of lattice gauge theories on quantum computers. Here, we consider regularizing the gauge field by replacing the gauge group $G$ with a braided fusion category whose objects correspond to Wilson lines of the associated Chern-Simons theory $G_k$, with the level $k$ serving as the regularization parameter. We demonstrate how to couple these regularized $U(1)$ and $SU(2)$ gauge groups to fermionic matter using the framework of fusion surface models, which treats matter and gauge field excitations as interacting anyons. We then address the simulation of the Hamiltonians we construct on fault-tolerant quantum computers, providing explicit quantum circuit constructions for implementing the primitive gates in this model, namely, the $F$ and $R$ symbols of the $U(1)_k$ and $SU(2)_k$ anyon theories, which may be of independent interest.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum simulation, lattice gauge theories, fermionic matter, anyonic regularization, fusion surface models, quantum circuits, Chern-Simons theory, fault-tolerant quantum computing

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究通过同时测量非简并放大器信号和闲频频率的双模压缩态，并在经典处理阶段相干组合以最大化信噪比，从而提高了超导量子比特的读取保真度。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 实现高保真度量子非破坏性量子比特读取能力，对于构建大规模高性能量子计算机至关重要。超导量子比特的此类读取通常通过使用保持相位的量子极限约瑟夫森放大器放大微弱色散测量信号来实现，该放大器需具备足够增益以稀释输出链引入的附加噪声贡献。本文中，我们通过以下方式进一步提升了量子比特读取保真度：（1）在非简并放大器的信号频率与闲频频率处，同时测量放大后读取信号的双模压缩态；（2）在经典处理阶段，对两路信号进行相对旋转以最大化量子比特编码读取正交分量的信噪比，随后对其进行相干合成。该读取方案在放大器增益与输出链附加噪声的所有实际取值范围内均展现出读取保真度的提升，且完全兼容大型量子处理器中采用的频率复用架构。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> The ability to perform high-fidelity quantum nondemolition qubit readout is pivotal for the realization of large and powerful quantum computers. Such readout of superconducting qubits is generally enabled by amplifying the weak dispersive measurement signals using phase-preserving quantum-limited Josephson amplifiers with sufficient gain to dilute the contribution of the added noise by the output chain. Here, we further enhance the qubit readout fidelity by (1) simultaneously measuring the two-mode squeezed states of the amplified readout signals at the signal and idler frequencies of the nondegenerate amplifier and (2) coherently combining them at the classical processing stage following a relative rotation that maximizes the signal to noise ratio of the qubit-encoded readout quadrature. Such readout scheme exhibits enhancement in the readout fidelity for all practical values of amplifier gain and noise added by the output chain and is fully compatible with frequency multiplexed setups used in large quantum processors.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: qubit readout fidelity, two-mode squeezing, superconducting qubits, quantum nondemolition measurement, Josephson amplifiers, signal-to-noise ratio, frequency multiplexed setups, quantum computers

### 253. ❌ Role of spectral structure in adiabatic ground-state preparation of the XXZ model

**作者**: Francisco Albarrán-Arriagada, Juan Carlos Retamal
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-16

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是量子物理中的XXZ模型（各向异性海森堡模型）的绝热基态制备问题，属于凝聚态物理和量子计算领域。论文内容涉及哈密顿量谱结构、能级交叉、绝热演化、反绝热驱动等物理概念，与医学图像分析、深度学习、疾病诊断、手术规划等医学人工智能领域完全无关。所有关键词均与论文主题无任何关联。

<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了XXZ模型中谱结构对绝热基态制备效率的影响，发现能级简并是主要限制因素，而通过优化初始哈密顿量或添加辅助场可以消除关键能级交叉，显著提高制备效率。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 绝热基态制备从根本上受限于含时哈密顿量的谱结构，特别是能隙缩小和简并所诱导的非绝热跃迁。我们通过比较三种策略——初始哈密顿量优化、添加辅助项以及考虑近似反绝热驱动——在八位点环上的各向异性海森堡（XXZ）模型中研究了这种依赖性。由于低能态间存在依赖于各向异性的能级交叉，XXZ模型提供了一个严格的基准。我们发现，制备性能主要受基态与激发态之间的谱简并所限制。诸如初始哈密顿量优化或位点依赖的塞曼场等简单策略，能够抑制关键交叉点并显著提升基态制备效率。相比之下，当谱结构中仍存在能级交叉时，仅靠反绝热项并不能改善制备效果，只有在简并被消除后这些项才变得有效。这些结果表明，谱工程是相互作用自旋系统中实现高效绝热基态制备的先决条件。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Adiabatic ground-state preparation is fundamentally limited by the spectral structure of the time-dependent Hamiltonian, particularly by gap reductions and degeneracies that induce nonadiabatic transitions. We examine this dependence in the anisotropic Heisenberg (XXZ) model on an eight-site ring by comparing three strategies: optimization of the initial Hamiltonian, addition of auxiliary terms, and considering approximate counterdiabatic driving. Owing to anisotropy-dependent level crossings among low-energy states, the XXZ model provides a stringent benchmark. We find that performance is mainly constrained by spectral degeneracies between the ground and excited states. Simple strategies such as initial-Hamiltonian optimization or site-dependent Zeeman fields, suppresses critical crossings and drastically enhance ground-state preparation. In contrast, counterdiabatic terms alone do not improve the protocol when the spectral structure remains level-crossings, becoming effective only after degeneracies are removed. These results identify spectral engineering as a prerequisite for efficient adiabatic ground-state preparation in interacting spin systems.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: adiabatic ground-state preparation, XXZ model, spectral structure, level crossings, Hamiltonian optimization, counterdiabatic driving, spin systems

### 254. ❌ Almost-iid information theory

**作者**: Giulia Mazzola, David Sutter, Renato Renner
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-16
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15792v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15792v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical image segmentation | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| AI for diagnosis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文《Almost-iid information theory》研究的是信息论中的基本理论问题，特别是关于几乎独立同分布（almost-iid）状态在信息处理任务中的有效性。论文内容完全属于理论信息论和量子信息论领域，涉及条件熵、压缩纠缠等理论概念，与医学图像分析、深度学习、疾病诊断、手术规划等临床医学应用没有任何关联。所有关键词均与医学图像或临床AI应用相关，而论文完全不涉及这些主题，因此所有关键词的相关度均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了几乎独立同分布（almost-iid）状态在信息处理任务中是否与完美独立同分布（iid）状态同样有效，并证明了几乎-iid状态的条件熵渐近地与iid状态的条件熵一致，从而表明压缩纠缠对于几乎-iid状态是稳健的。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 信息论技术基于资源可由独立同分布状态充分表征的假设。这一假设在操作上无法被证明合理，因为例如，源发射的后续系统间的相关性无法通过任何实际的层析成像协议检测到。由操作动机驱动的对称性假设，通过德菲内蒂定理，仍意味着资源可由近似独立同分布状态描述。这引出一个问题：对于信息处理任务而言，近似独立同分布资源是否与完美独立同分布资源同样有效？本文探讨此问题，并证明近似独立同分布状态的条件熵在渐近意义上与独立同分布状态的条件熵一致。作为应用，这意味着压缩纠缠对于近似独立同分布状态具有鲁棒性，其值在渐近意义上与在独立同分布状态上的取值相符。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Information-theoretic techniques are based on the assumption that resources are well characterized by independent and identically distributed (iid) states. This assumption cannot be justified operationally, since, for example, correlations between subsequent systems emitted by a source cannot be detected by any practical tomographic protocol. Operationally motivated symmetry assumptions still imply, via de Finetti theorems, that the resources are described by almost-iid states. This raises the question: Are almost-iid resources as effective as perfect iid resources for information-processing tasks? Here we address this question and prove that the conditional entropy of almost-iid states asymptotically coincides with that of iid states. As an application, this implies that squashed entanglement is robust for almost-iid states, asymptotically matching its value on iid states.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: information theory, almost-iid states, conditional entropy, squashed entanglement, de Finetti theorems, asymptotic analysis, quantum information processing

---

### 255. ❌ Hubbard model at U=$\infty$: Role of single and two-boson fluctuations

**作者**: Debanand Sa, Anirban Dutta
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-16
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15790v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15790v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了U=∞ Hubbard模型中强关联电子系统的性质，通过半解析框架计算了费米子自能和玻色子谱密度，发现电阻率在宽温度范围内呈线性依赖并在极低温下过渡到相干费米液体行为。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们开发了一种基于正则费米子表述的半解析框架，用以研究强关联电子体系。我们考虑U=$\infty$的哈伯德模型，并采用运动方程方法计算费米子自能。该自能包含两部分：单玻色子交换过程与双玻色子交换过程。其中涌现的玻色子来源于体系自生的局域电荷与自旋密度涨落，这些涨落由于极端关联效应而表现出强烈的时间依赖性。计算得到的玻色子谱密度呈现为具有长尾特征的扩散阻尼模式。在$d=\infty$维度下，我们自洽地计算了电子自能。相应的费米子谱密度在$ω=0$处显示出一个显著的相干峰，而其频率导数在有限$ω$处呈现出双峰结构。电阻率在较宽温度范围内表现出线性温度依赖性，并在极低温下过渡到相干的费米液体行为。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We have developed a semi-analytical framework formulated in the canonical fermion representation to investigate strongly correlated electron systems. We consider the U=$\infty$ Hubbard model and used the equation of motion method to calculate the fermion self-energy which has two parts: single and two-boson exchange processes. The emergent bosons here are self-generated local charge and spin-density fluctuations which become strongly time-dependent due to extreme correlations. The computed boson spectral density is a diffusive damped mode with a long tail. The electron self-energy at $d=\infty$ is computed self-consistently. The corresponding fermionic spectral density displays a pronounced coherence peak at $ω=0$, while its frequency derivative develops a two-peak structure at finite $ω$. The resistivity shows a linear temperature dependence over a broad range, crossing over to coherent Fermi-liquid behavior at extremely low temperatures.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: Hubbard model, strongly correlated electron systems, fermion self-energy, boson fluctuations, spectral density, resistivity, canonical fermion representation, equation of motion method

### 256. ❌ Physics-informed neural networks for solving strong-field saddle-point equations in strong-field physics with tailored fields

**作者**: Jiakang Chen, Sufia Hashim, Carla Figueira de Morisson Faria
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-16
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15786v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15786v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 该论文研究的是强场物理中的鞍点方程求解问题，使用物理信息神经网络（PINN）解决强场近似下的直接阈上电离问题。论文内容完全属于物理学领域，涉及激光物理、强场物理、计算物理和机器学习应用。所有评分关键词均来自医学图像分析和临床决策支持领域，与论文的物理学研究内容无任何关联。论文未涉及医学图像、医疗诊断、手术规划或任何医疗应用。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文开发了一种基于物理信息神经网络的求解器，用于解决强场物理中鞍点方程的计算问题，成功恢复了复杂电离时间并计算了光电子动量分布，为半经典强场计算提供了新框架。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们开发了一种无监督的物理信息神经网络，用于求解强场近似下直接阈上电离所遵循的鞍点方程。该框架提供了一个结构清晰的理论测试平台，其中针对特定设计的驱动场，其鞍点结构已知，从而能够对所提出的求解器进行系统性验证。在此方法中，网络通过最小化鞍点方程的残差进行训练，仅需定义驱动场的波形及其参数，如强度、载波包络相位、椭圆率和相对相位。我们引入了一种窗口参数化策略，将网络输出映射到复时间平面的指定区域，从而引导优化过程朝向物理相关的解，并提高了收敛稳定性。我们针对一系列驱动场，将物理信息神经网络与传统求解器进行了基准测试，结果表明该网络能够在较宽的参数范围内稳健地恢复主导的复电离时间。随着激光参数的变化，网络能够追踪电离事件主导性的改变，从而得以探索那些传统求解器需要反复手动初始化的参数区域。利用物理信息神经网络得到的解，我们计算了相干阈上电离光电子动量分布，并展示了驱动场的对称性同时反映在鞍点结构和所得谱图中。这些结果确立了物理信息神经网络作为半经典强场计算的一个有前景的框架，并为将机器学习求解器扩展至库仑修正模型或更复杂的物理过程（如再散射阈上电离）奠定了基础。对于后者，其鞍点方程具有高度非线性，且存在多个间距很近的解，这使得传统的牛顿型求根法对初始猜测高度敏感，从而阻碍了在激光参数空间（尤其是针对定制场）进行系统性研究。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We develop an unsupervised physics-informed neural network to solve saddle-point equations governing direct above-threshold ionization within the strong-field approximation. This setting provides a well-understood testbed in which the saddle-point structure is known for tailored driving fields, enabling systematic validation of the proposed solver. In this approach, the network is trained by minimizing the residual of the SPEs and requires only the definition of the driving-field shape and its parameters, such as intensity, carrier-envelope phase, ellipticity, and relative phase. We introduce a window parametrization strategy that maps network outputs to prescribed regions of the complex-time plane, guiding the optimization toward physically relevant solutions and improving convergence stability. We benchmark the PINN against a conventional solver for a range of fields, demonstrating robust recovery of the dominant complex ionization times over wide parameter ranges. The network tracks changes in ionization event dominance as laser parameters are varied, enabling exploration of regimes where conventional solvers require repeated manual initialization. Using the PINN-derived solutions, we compute coherent ATI photoelectron momentum distributions and show the symmetries of the driving fields are reflected in both the saddle-point structure and the resulting spectra. These results establish PINNs as a promising framework for semiclassical strong-field calculations and provide a foundation for extending machine-learning solvers to Coulomb-corrected models or to more complex processes, such as rescattered ATI for which the SPEs are highly nonlinear and the presence of multiple closely-spaced solutions makes conventional Newton-type root-finding highly sensitive to initial guesses, which hinders systematic investigations across laser-parameter spaces, particularly for tailored fields.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: physics-informed neural networks, strong-field physics, saddle-point equations, above-threshold ionization, complex ionization times, laser parameters, photoelectron momentum distributions, machine-learning solvers

### 257. ❌ Latent symmetry in a minimal non-Hermitian trimer

**作者**: Paulo A. Brandão

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是非厄米三聚体系统中的潜在对称性、PT对称性和异常点物理，属于理论物理和量子物理领域，与医学图像分析、人工智能临床决策支持等医学应用完全无关。所有关键词均未在标题或摘要中出现，也没有任何间接关联。

<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了一个具有潜在对称性的最小非厄米三聚体模型，证明了其可分解为暗态和亮态两个部分，其中亮态子系统在特定参数下呈现PT对称性并包含一个嵌入的二阶异常点，从而实现了潜在对称性、PT对称性和异常点物理的自然共存。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们研究了一个具有潜在对称性的最小非厄米三聚体模型，该模型由嵌入在具有非互易耦合的三节点网络中的一对共谱节点构成。研究表明，该模型可精确分解为暗态与亮态子空间：暗模式在谱上孤立且保持复本征值，而亮态部分约化为一个有效的非厄米二聚体子系统。在适当参数选择下，该简化子系统呈现$\mathcal{PT}$对称性，并展现出部分谱实性——两个实本征值与暗态的复本征值共存。在临界点处，亮态子空间包含一个嵌入的二阶奇异点，使得完整三聚体系统出现缺陷态，并产生典型的约当块动力学行为。这些结果确立了该非厄米三聚体作为一个最小解析可解模型，其中潜在对称性、子空间分辨的$\mathcal{PT}$对称性与奇异点物理机制得以自然共存。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We study a minimal non-Hermitian trimer with latent symmetry formed by a cospectral pair of sites embedded in a three-site network with nonreciprocal couplings. We show that the model admits an exact decomposition into dark and bright sectors: the dark mode is spectrally isolated and retains a complex eigenvalue, while the bright sector reduces to an effective non-Hermitian dimer. For a suitable choice of parameters, this reduced subsystem becomes $\mathcal{PT}$-symmetric and exhibits partial spectral reality, with two real eigenvalues coexisting with the complex dark eigenvalue. At the critical point, the bright sector hosts an embedded second-order exceptional point, which renders the full trimer defective and gives rise to the characteristic Jordan-block dynamics. These results establish the non-Hermitian trimer as a minimal analytically solvable setting in which latent symmetry, sector-resolved $\mathcal{PT}$ symmetry, and exceptional-point physics naturally coexist.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: non-Hermitian trimer, latent symmetry, PT symmetry, exceptional point, spectral decomposition, dark mode, bright sector, Jordan-block dynamics

### 258. ❌ A fault-tolerant encoding for qubit-controlled collective spins

**作者**: Charlotte Franke, Dorian A. Gangloff
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-16
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15760v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15760v1)

| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究量子计算中的量子纠错编码（spin-N-Cat codes），属于量子物理和量子信息领域，与医学图像分析、人工智能临床决策支持等关键词完全无关。论文内容涉及量子点、自旋系统、量子纠错等，未提及任何医学影像、疾病诊断或医疗应用。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种名为spin-N-Cat codes的量子纠错编码方法，用于自旋系统量子计算，通过一阶相互作用实现高效、容错的逻辑门操作，显著延长了量子相干时间。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 量子纠错（QEC）对于可扩展的量子计算不可或缺，但以最小的硬件开销实现它仍是一个核心挑战。具有集体自由度的大自旋系统为降低量子比特架构的控制复杂度提供了一条有前景的路径，同时保留了用于容错编码的大希尔伯特空间。然而，目前针对自旋系综中逻辑门和量子纠错的方案通常依赖于低效的高阶相互作用。本文我们提出了自旋-N-猫态编码，该编码将逻辑量子比特编码在自旋相干态的叠加态中，并将玻色猫态编码推广到置换对称自旋系综的模子空间。该编码能够纠正集体和个体的退相位、激发与衰减错误。我们还提出了一种在中心自旋系统（如量子点）中的高效物理实现方案，其中编码、解码以及一套通用的、容错的、且保持偏置特性的门集合仅需使用一阶相互作用即可实现。数值模拟表明，在退相位和激发-衰减噪声下，该编码具有较高的逻辑保真度，且与噪声偏置无关；同时，完整的量子纠错循环在现实的微观参数下是可行的。对于量子点中可用的大集体自旋而言，这相当于显著地延长了相干时间。我们的研究结果确立了自旋-N-猫态编码作为一种可扩展、硬件高效的量子纠错方法，适用于基于自旋的量子架构。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Quantum error correction (QEC) is indispensable for scalable quantum computing, but implementing it with minimal hardware overhead remains a central challenge. Large spin systems with collective degrees of freedom offer a promising route to reducing the control complexity of qubit architectures while retaining a large Hilbert space for fault-tolerant encoding. However, existing proposals for logical gates and QEC in spin ensembles generally rely on inefficient higher-order interactions. Here we introduce spin-N-Cat codes, which encode logical qubits in superpositions of spin-coherent states and generalize bosonic Cat codes to the modular subspaces of permutationally symmetric spin ensembles. The code corrects collective and individual dephasing, excitation, and decay errors. We also present an efficient physical realization in central-spin systems, such as a quantum dot, where encoding, decoding, and a universal, fault-tolerant, and bias-preserving gate set are implemented using only first-order interactions. Numerical simulations demonstrate high logical fidelity under dephasing and excitation-decay noise, independent of noise bias, and that full QEC cycles are feasible with realistic microscopic parameters. For the large collective spins available in quantum dots, this translates into a substantial extension of coherence time. Our results establish spin-N-Cat codes as a scalable, hardware-efficient approach to QEC in spin-based quantum architectures.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum error correction, spin-N-Cat codes, fault-tolerant encoding, central-spin systems, quantum dot, logical qubits, collective spins, QEC cycles

### 259. ❌ Quantum Noise Suppression at Scale with Crosstalk-Robust Gate Sets

**期刊/来源**: arxiv

**评分理由**: 论文研究量子计算中的噪声抑制和门集优化，涉及量子最优控制、量子硬件-软件协同设计、量子算法性能提升等，属于量子物理和量子计算领域。所有评分关键词均围绕医学影像分析和临床AI应用，与论文主题完全无关，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种通过量子最优控制设计抗串扰门集的方法，以抑制量子噪声并提升量子算法的性能，在IBM量子平台上验证了该方法可将算法性能中值提升四倍，并可能将双量子比特门时间减半。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们引入了一种抗串扰门集，该门集通过利用局域性的新型可扩展最优控制问题实现。通过抑制两两量子串扰，该门集能够将鲁棒性扩展至多量子比特电路。IBM量子平台设备为我们的门集提供了测试环境，我们通过误差抑制协议和最多八个量子比特的随机并行单量子比特电路研究了其效能。此外，我们首次评估了完整最优控制门集对量子算法的影响。通过对四量子比特横向场伊辛模型进行哈密顿量模拟，我们证明在相同校准流程下，噪声感知门将算法中位性能较基线高斯门提升了四倍。最后，我们提供了数值证据，表明优化后的门集能够实现更大的量子比特间耦合强度，从而将双量子比特门时间减半。这一结果证实了基于量子最优控制的硬件-软件协同设计能够为量子计算架构创造新的机遇。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We introduce crosstalk-robust gate sets, which are obtained using a novel, scalable optimal control problem exploiting locality. Through the suppression of pairwise quantum crosstalk, the gate sets enable robustness that extends to multi-qubit circuits. The IBM Quantum Platform devices provide a testbed for our gate sets, where we study their efficacy via error suppression protocols and randomized parallel single-qubit circuits of up to eight qubits. Furthermore, we provide the first known assessment of the impact of complete optimal control gate sets on quantum algorithms. Using a Hamiltonian simulation of a four-qubit transverse field Ising model, we show that noise-informed gates enhance median algorithmic performance by a factor of four over baseline Gaussian gates using the same calibration procedures. Lastly, we provide numerical evidence that optimized gate sets enable larger qubit-qubit coupling strengths that can cut two-qubit gate times in half. This result confirms that hardware-software co-design using quantum optimal control can create new opportunities for quantum computing architectures.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum noise suppression, crosstalk-robust gate sets, quantum optimal control, quantum computing, IBM Quantum Platform, Hamiltonian simulation, hardware-software co-design, quantum algorithms

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究针对量子HHL算法在近期量子模拟器上的实现进行优化，通过Suzuki-Trotter分解和块编码方法改进保真度和可扩展性，发现算法性能受矩阵稀疏度影响显著，结构化矩阵表现接近理想而稠密矩阵性能下降。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> Harrow-Hassidim-Lloyd（HHL）算法是一种用于求解线性方程组的量子算法，原则上相比经典方法，其在系统规模扩展上可提供指数级加速。本研究聚焦于在近期量子模拟器上提升HHL算法的实际性能，探讨了其实施与优化方案。在概述算法原理后，我们研究了两种旨在提高保真度与可扩展性的优化策略：哈密顿演化算符的Suzuki-Trotter分解，以及将问题矩阵嵌入更大幺正算符的块编码方法。通过在不同稀疏度矩阵（包括对角矩阵、三对角矩阵、中等密度矩阵及完全稠密矩阵）上进行仿真，评估了这些方法的性能。结果表明，虽然HHL对高度结构化的矩阵能实现接近理想的保真度，但随着稀疏度降低，由于哈密顿模拟成本增加以及条件数升高导致的后选择概率下降，其性能会逐渐恶化。研究发现，块编码方法对中等密度矩阵能提供更高的保真度，而Trotter分解则为稀疏系统提供了一种量子比特效率较高的实现途径。这些结果凸显了矩阵结构对决定HHL实际效率的重要性，并为未来结合算法优化与硬件感知设计的实施方案提供了参考。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> The Harrow-Hassidim-Lloyd (HHL) algorithm is a quantum algorithm for solving systems of linear equations that, in principle, offers an exponential improvement in scaling with the system size compared to classical approaches. In this work, we investigate the practical implementation and optimisation of the HHL algorithm with a focus on improving its performance on near-term quantum simulators. After outlining the algorithm, we examine two optimisation strategies aimed at improving fidelity and scalability: Suzuki-Trotter decomposition of the Hamiltonian evolution operator and a block-encoding approach that embeds the problem matrix into a larger unitary operator. The performance of these methods is evaluated through simulations on matrices with varying sparsity, including diagonal, tridiagonal, moderately dense, and fully dense cases. Our results show that while HHL achieves near-ideal fidelity for highly structured matrices, performance degrades as sparsity decreases due to the increasing cost of Hamiltonian simulation and reduced post-selection probability due to higher condition number. Block encoding is found to provide improved fidelity for moderately dense matrices, whereas Trotterisation offers a qubit-efficient approach for sparse systems. These results highlight the importance of matrix structure in determining the practical efficiency of HHL and inform future implementations that combine algorithmic optimisation with hardware-aware design.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: HHL algorithm, quantum algorithm, linear equations, Hamiltonian evolution, Suzuki-Trotter decomposition, block encoding, quantum simulation, matrix sparsity

### 261. ❌ Can quantum fluctuations be consistently monitored?

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了量子多体系统中宏观量波动的一致监测问题，发现除无限温度、临界点和半经典系统等特殊情况外，波动一般无法被一致监测，并用量化非一致性分析了熵增长。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 近期关于退相干历史形式体系的研究表明，量子多体系统中的宏观量（局域可观测量的大范围求和）可以被一致性地监测：过往测量的存在不会改变未来结果的概率分布。本文指出，与宏观量的强度均值不同，其涨落通常无法被一致性地监测。例外情形包括无限温度下的涨落、临界点处的涨落以及半经典系统中的涨落。我们通过磁化率解析量化了非一致性程度，并获得了噪声幺正演化下熵增长的相关结果。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Recent works on the decoherent histories formalism suggested that macroscopic quantities (extensive sums of local observables) in quantum many-body systems can be consistently monitored: The existence of past measurements does not alter future outcome distribution. Here, we show that fluctuations of macroscopic quantities cannot be consistently monitored in general, in contrast to their intensive mean value. Exceptions include fluctuations at infinite temperature, at critical points, and in semiclassical systems. We analytically quantify non-consistency in terms of susceptibility, and obtain related results on entropy growth under noisy unitary.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum fluctuations, decoherent histories, macroscopic quantities, quantum many-body systems, susceptibility, entropy growth, noisy unitary

### 262. ❌ Post-selected Criticality in Measurement-induced Phase Transitions

**作者**: Dolly Nambi, Kabir Khanna, Andrew Allocca, Thomas Iadecola, Ciarán Hickey, Romain Vasseur, Justin H. Wilson
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-16
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15744v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15744v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical image segmentation | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| AI for diagnosis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是量子物理中的测量诱导相变（MIPT），属于量子信息、凝聚态物理领域，涉及量子电路、后选择测量、普适性分类、纠缠转变等概念。所有评分关键词均围绕医学影像分析、人工智能辅助临床决策，包括医学图像分割、深度学习医学成像、AI诊断、预后预测、手术规划、多模态医学成像、医学影像基础模型等。论文内容与这些医学领域关键词完全无关，没有任何医学影像、临床数据或医疗应用的内容，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了后选择如何改变测量诱导相变的普适性类别，发现后选择通过重新加权罕见轨迹改变了相变性质，并确定了与随机张量网络相同的普适性类别。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 信息论相变，例如测量诱导相变，表征了量子动力学对局域监控的鲁棒性，其自然表述基于典型测量结果所对应的轨迹，而这些轨迹通常只能通过后选择来获取。本文通过实施强制测量，研究了显式的后选择如何改变相变的性质。我们发现，后选择通过对原本稀有的轨迹进行重新加权，从根本上改变了普适性类。具体而言，我们获得了大于标准测量诱导相变的相关长度指数 $ν\approx 2.1$，以及负的有效中心荷 $c_\mathrm{eff}\approx -0.4$。我们还将后选择的测量诱导相变与随机张量网络的纠缠相变进行了比较，并证明它们属于同一普适性类。此实验设置进一步允许研究具有后选择弱测量的时间周期、平移不变电路。在这两种模型中，我们发现至少需要3维的局域希尔伯特空间（即量子三态系统而非量子比特）才能诱发相变。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Information-theoretic phase transitions, such as the measurement-induced phase transition (MIPT), characterize the robustness of quantum dynamics to local monitoring and are naturally formulated in terms of trajectories conditioned on typical measurement outcomes, which are naively accessible only through post-selection. Here we implement forced measurements to investigate how explicit post-selection alters the nature of the transition. We find that post-selection fundamentally alters the universality class by reweighting trajectories that are otherwise rare. In particular, we obtain a correlation-length exponent $ν\approx 2.1$ larger than that of the standard MIPT and a negative effective central charge $c_\mathrm{eff}\approx -0.4$. We also compare the post-selected MIPT to the entanglement transition of Random Tensor Networks (RTN), and demonstrate that their universality class is the same. This setup further allows time-periodic, translationally-invariant circuits with post-selected weak measurements. In both models, we find that an onsite dimension of at least 3 (qutrits but not qubits) is necessary to induce a transition.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: measurement-induced phase transition, post-selection, universality class, quantum circuits, entanglement transition, Random Tensor Networks, critical exponents

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 在退相干理论中，冗余性是指量子系统与环境各部分之间的关联性，它是经典行为涌现的基础。我们证明，即使环境存在热化动力学，冗余性仍可得以维持。这一结论源于初始的广播相互作用，该作用改变了守恒量的密度。我们利用主导子系统热化的大偏差原理，估算了系统与环境部分之间的互信息。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> In the theory of decoherence, redundancy is the correlation between a quantum system and fractions of the environment. It underlies the emergence of classical behavior. We show that redundancy can persist despite thermalizing dynamics in the environment. This follows an initial broadcasting interaction that changes the density of a conserved quantity. The mutual information between the system and a fraction of the environment is estimated using the large deviation principle governing subsystem thermalization.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: redundancy, decoherence, quantum system, thermalizing dynamics, subsystem thermalization, large deviation principle, mutual information, environment

### 264. ❌ Entanglement advantage in sensing power-law spatiotemporal noise correlations

**作者**: Yu-Xin Wang, Anthony J. Brady, Federico Belliardo, Alexey V. Gorshkov

**评分理由**: 论文研究量子传感器在探测时空相关噪声中的纠缠优势，属于量子物理、量子传感和量子信息领域。所有评分关键词均涉及医学影像分析、人工智能在医疗中的应用，与论文的量子物理主题完全无关。论文未涉及任何医学影像、深度学习、疾病诊断、手术规划或多模态医疗数据。
